Tax Reduction Plan of Japanese Government Party

Seiyukai Believes it is Clumsy Propaganda

Minseito Dissatisfied with Hamaguchi's Attitude

Denyusha, Tokyo, 4th - The Seiyukai Executive Committee held a meeting yesterday at the Seiyukai headquarters. At the meeting, the general affairs criticized the tax reduction plan of the government and the party, saying that the naval expenditure for the established expenditure for the Showa 5th and 6th years must be 165 million yen. Afterwards, there will be subsidies for the construction of warships and the replacement construction of submarines every year, which must also cost more than 70 million yen. Furthermore, in order to eliminate the defense anxiety caused by the London Treaty, the air force must be expanded, which will also cost a lot of money. It is bound to use the surplus funds from military reduction. It can be seen that the government's statement that the result of military reduction is used for tax reduction is completely false. It is a clumsy propaganda of the government and the party to deceive the people.

Denyusha, Tokyo, 4th - Three people, including Minseito general affairs Sakurauchi Yukio, visited Prime Minister Hamaguchi yesterday as representatives of the party and requested that the surplus funds from the national treasury resulting from military reduction be used as a source of tax reduction to implement the policy of the Minseito. Prime Minister Hamaguchi replied that the surplus funds from military reduction cannot be used for purposes other than the necessary naval-related expenditures. The young and middle-aged members of the Minseito were dissatisfied with the Prime Minister's statement that the policy of using the surplus funds puts naval expenditure first and tax reduction second, forgetting the meaning of military reduction, which is to reduce the burden on the people. They were all dissatisfied with the Prime Minister's attitude of exclusively relying on the Navy's breath.

Graf Zeppelin Flies Back to Europe

Scheduled Transatlantic Air Route

Preparation to Open Next Autumn

National Society, Friedrichshafen, 3rd - The Graf Zeppelin airship returned to Europe from the United States on Tuesday at midnight. More than 100,000 people came to see it off. In addition to a large number of mails, the ship carried 22 passengers. It is reported that Dr. Eckener announced before the ship's departure that a scheduled transatlantic air route would be opened next fall, with one flight every five days.

National Society, Lakehurst, 3rd - According to the wireless telegraph sent by the Graf Zeppelin airship today, it is currently proceeding towards Seville, Spain. At 5:00 AM this morning, it had reached a space 552 miles east of New York.

National Society, New York, 3rd - According to the wireless telegraph this afternoon, the Graf Zeppelin airship is flying at an average speed of one mile per minute due to favorable winds.

Italian Foreign Minister Delivers Speech in the Upper House

To Promote the Effectiveness of the League of Nations Charter

It is Necessary to First Seek International Goodwill

National Society, Rome, 3rd - Italian Foreign Minister Grandi delivered an extraordinary speech in the Upper House today. After declaring that Italy had made the most progress in the London Naval Reduction Conference and repeatedly reiterating the Italian-French naval equality requirements, he discussed Briand's Pan-European Conference plan, believing that if European countries could trust and be more friendly with each other, this plan would be more valuable. He also said that in order to promote the effectiveness of the League of Nations Charter, it is necessary to first seek the goodwill of nations. Italy will strive to achieve this in the future. He believes that European problems should be resolved in the following order: first, reduce armaments; second, arbitrate; and finally, guarantee security.

Reuters, London, 3rd - Italian Foreign Minister Grandi said in the Senate today regarding the naval treaty that Italy is prepared to suspend the 1930 naval construction program while matters unresolved at the London Naval Conference are pending negotiation, but France must also do the same.

National Society, Winnipeg, 3rd - A forest fire broke out on the border of northern Ontario, burning for more than 200 miles. Residents in the surrounding area are fleeing south. The calculated number of people in difficulty is still different from the original number, probably because they had difficulty walking and were buried in the fire. Firefighters used airplanes as guidance, sending signals from the air so that they could rush to the rescue as directed by the signals. However, countless beautiful trees have been burned.

Japanese Emperor's Brother Arrives in Paris on the 3rd

Important News

Zhejiang Province Disaster Relief Bond Regulations Passed by the Legislative Yuan

The following are the Zhejiang Province Disaster Relief Bond Regulations passed by the Legislative Yuan at its 93rd meeting on the 31st of last month: (Article 1) The Zhejiang Provincial Government shall issue disaster relief bonds for the purpose of providing disaster relief in the province in the amount of 1 million national currency, designated as the Zhejiang Province Disaster Relief Bonds of the Republic of China, 1920 (Article 2) The annual interest rate of this bond shall be set at 8% (Article 3) This bond shall be issued at 98% of its face value (Article 4) This bond shall be issued on July 1, 1920 (Article 5) This bond shall pay interest twice a year, at the end of June and the end of December (Article 6) This bond shall be redeemed by lottery starting in December 1920 over a period of nine years. A lottery shall be held twice a year until the end of June 1928, when the principal and interest shall be fully repaid. The aforementioned lottery shall be held on June 15 and December 15 each year, and payment shall commence at the end of the same month (Article 7) The number of bonds to be drawn in each lottery and the amount of principal and interest to be repaid shall be in accordance with the provisions of the principal and interest repayment schedule (Article 8) The Zhejiang Provincial Government shall allocate 160,000 national currency annually from the stamp duty revenue to serve as a fund for repaying principal and interest on this bond (Article 9) The bond fund shall be specially deposited in the Zhejiang Local Bank and managed by the Bond Fund Management Committee. The aforementioned Bond Fund Management Committee shall be composed of two members appointed by the Provincial Government and one member each recommended by the Hangzhou General Chamber of Commerce, the Banking Association, and the Money Industry Association. The management rules shall be separately determined (Article 10) This bond shall be available in denominations of 1,000 yuan, 100 yuan, and 10 yuan, all of which shall be in unregistered form (Article 11) The Zhejiang Local Bank and the governments of various cities and counties shall be the management agencies for this bond's principal and interest repayment (Article 12) Bonds and matured interest coupons drawn for this bond may be used to pay all taxes in the province (Article 13) This bond may be freely bought and sold or mortgaged. It may be used as collateral when depositing security deposits for official business, and may be used as guarantee reserves for banks (Article 14) Anyone who forges or damages the credit of this bond shall be punished by the judicial authorities in accordance with the law (Article 15) These regulations shall take effect from the date of promulgation

Revised Organic Law of the Executive Yuan

Passed by the 93rd Meeting of the Legislative Yuan

The Organic Law of the Executive Yuan has been revised by the 93rd meeting of the Legislative Yuan. The original text is recorded as follow: (Article 1) The Executive Yuan shall be organized by the following ministries and committees: (1) Ministry of Interior (2) Ministry of Foreign Affairs (3) Ministry of Military Affairs (4) Ministry of the Navy (5) Ministry of Finance (6) Ministry of Agriculture and Mining (7) Ministry of Industry and Commerce (8) Ministry of Education (9) Ministry of Transportation (10) Ministry of Railways (11) Ministry of Health (12) Construction Committee (13) Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission (14) Labor Committee (15) Anti-Smoking Committee (Article 2) The Executive Yuan may, with the deliberation and decision of the State Council and the Legislative Yuan, increase, merge, or abolish various ministries, committees, and other agencies (Article 3) The President shall direct all the Yuan's affairs and its subordinate agencies (Article 4) The Executive Yuan shall have the following offices: (1) Secretariat (2) Political Affairs Office (Article 5) The Secretariat shall have the following officials: (1) Secretary-General, one person, appointed (2) Secretaries, six to ten people, four of whom are appointed, and the rest are recommended (3) Clerks, ten to twenty people, appointed, but four of them may be recommended (Article 6) The Secretariat shall be in charge of the following matters: (1) Matters concerning the receipt, dispatch, compilation, and storage of documents (2) Matters concerning the distribution of documents (3) Matters concerning the drafting and translation of documents (4) Matters concerning the appointment and removal of officials appointed by this Yuan (5) Matters concerning the custody of seals (6) Matters concerning accounting and general affairs (7) Other matters not under the jurisdiction of the Political Affairs Office (Article 7) The Political Affairs Office shall have the following officials: (1) Director of Political Affairs Office, one person, appointed (2) Councillors, four to six people, appointed (3) Clerks, ten to twenty people, appointed, but six of them may be recommended (Article 8) The Political Affairs Office shall be in charge of the following matters: (1) Matters concerning the meetings of this Yuan (2) Matters concerning matters to be submitted to the State Council or decided by the State Council and sent to this Yuan (3) Matters concerning matters to be submitted to the Legislative Yuan or sent to this Yuan by the Legislative Yuan (4) Matters concerning appeals (5) Matters concerning the drafting of orders, but not those under the jurisdiction of the Secretariat (Article 9) The for the offices shall be determined separately (Article 11) This law shall take effect from the date of promulgation

The Battle Situation on the Pinghan Railway

The Central Army's Right Wing Attacks Qixian

The Central Route Army Passes Linying and Encircles Xuchang

Yancheng Correspondence, June 1st. The Central Army on the Pinghan Railway is achieving successive victories. Apart from the somewhat subdued news from the left wing, the two divisions on the right wing are bravely advancing, bypassing Zhoujiakou from Queshan and Yancheng in a matter of ten days, heading north, passing Xihua, Taikang, and Suixian, and approaching Qixian. This area is defended by the forces of Sun Liangcheng and Ji Hongchang, who are confronting the Central Army at Wuji, ten miles from the city. A fierce battle has been raging since May 24th for eight days and nights, eventually leading to the Central Army's occupation. They are now attacking Qixian to link up with the Central Army on the Longhai Railway and directly seize Lanfeng. The central route has already passed Linying and is besieging Xuchang, which is expected to fall soon. When Linying was captured, the residents of the city, resentful of the harsh levies imposed by Fan Zhongxiu's troops for a long time, actively bound up and handed over any remaining Fan soldiers who had not managed to escape the city to be dealt with when the Central Army entered the city. On the evening of May 31st, Feng's troops were tightening the siege on Xuchang while also dispatching a small number of troops to harass the left wing to divide their forces. The sound of cannons roared loudly all night long. They were repelled by Xu Yuanquan's troops, and it is reported that Feng's troops suffered heavy casualties.

Guangdong Expeditionary Force Arrives at the Hunan Border

Guangzhou Correspondence. The Zhang Gui troops' abandonment of Guangxi and entry into Hunan have recently led to their arrival between Hengyang and Yongzhou. According to news from the front on the 26th, these Zhang Gui troops are still hovering around Hengyang, and whether they will take a detour through Hengshan to attack Zhuzhou and Liling remains to be seen. Therefore, the Guangdong pursuing troops are swiftly intensifying their departure. The authorities have ordered the completion of the transportation of the northbound troops by the end of May, gradually concentrating them on the Hunan border to await orders. It is reported that the Third Independent Brigade of the Sixth Route Army, commanded by Xu Kexiang, has also been ordered to return to the province from Wuzhou, taking the North River route to Hunan. Jiang Guangnai is leading two divisions of elite troops into Hunan, and preparations of all kinds are being made very thoroughly. In addition to the expeditionary force's expenses already being disbursed by the Finance Department, the headquarters yesterday also established supply stations and branch supervisory offices in Shaozhou, Lechang, and other places to facilitate the transportation of military supplies, and added a North River military long-distance telephone line, which was first established from Guangzhou through Shaoguan and Lechang to Chenzhou. Furthermore, two new teams of military communications units have recently been formed, and ten military telegraph operators have been selected and appointed from the Guangzhou Telegraph Bureau to be divided into two groups to accompany the Jiang and Cai divisions into Hunan. In addition, the air force is also a major force in pursuing the enemy into Hunan. On the 26th, Deng Yueming, the captain of the Second Air Squadron of the Aviation Department, led planes and flew to the Hengyang area to scout out the enemy's whereabouts, and will join the army in encircling and attacking the enemy when the army reaches the enemy's defense line. Jiang Guangnai, the commander-in-chief of the forward forces, led personnel from the 61st Division into Hunan from Shaozhou on the 27th to arrive at the Hunan border before the 31st, and will order a push south into Hunan as soon as all the divisions have arrived in Chenzhou. The direction of the advance will depend on the whereabouts of the Zhang Gui troops. (May 30th)

Reasons for the Decline of Qingdao's Fishing Industry

Qingdao Correspondence. The coastal area of Shandong has always been known as the richest fishing area, and the Jiaozhou Bay area is particularly prominent due to its shallow inland waters and numerous beaches. However, in recent years, fishermen have continued to use old methods and have not sought to improve them, and the authorities have not promoted or supported them, allowing the industry to decline, causing a great fishing area to fall into decline. Japanese fishermen have seized the opportunity to invade our territorial waters and seize our fishing rights, which is truly regrettable. The investigation of the fishing industry situation is as follows:

Investigation of Coastal Fishing Grounds: (1) Dengyao Port is located south of Dengyao Village in the Shazikou District, about seventy miles from Qingdao. Fishing was very prosperous here in the spring and winter seasons in the past. Fishermen from Qingshan and Huangshan in Jimo also used this place as a sales market. Now, there are very few fishermen fishing there, and it is no longer worthy of being called a fishing port. (2) Shazikou is located east of Qingdao, about sixty miles away, and is the most prosperous fishing port in the entire district. The port can be divided into three areas: Shazikou, Haimiao Bay, and Quanziya (i.e., Jianggezhuang Bay). This port is the center for offshore fishing, and the amount of fish produced is the highest in the entire district. (3) Shilaoren Bay is located west of Shazikou, about forty miles from Qingdao. The bay is mostly rocky and not very deep. Only in the spring are hairtail caught here. (4) Shandongtou Bay is located west of Shilaoren, about thirty-five miles from Qingdao. The most cuttlefish are caught in this bay during the spring season. During the remaining period, miscellaneous fish are caught by fishing. (5) Xiaogang (also known as Qingdao Port) is located southeast of the Taitung District, about thirty miles from Qingdao. The most hairtail and mullet are produced during the spring season. (6) Sifang Lake Island and other places used to have a fishing ground, but it has now disappeared due to the influence of factories. (7) Shalingzhuang Houwan is located north of Shalingzhuang in the Sifang District, about thirty-five miles from Qingdao. There were still fishermen fishing here twenty years ago, but now the fishing ground has disappeared due to the influence of factories. (8) Cangkou Bay is located north of Qingdao, about thirty miles from Qingdao. Thirty years ago, it was still a fishing ground, but today fishermen mostly go to outside ports. However, there are still many merchant ships coming here in the autumn to load fruits. (9) Nvgushan Bay is located north of Cangkou, about forty-five miles from Qingdao. The most clams, cockles, etc. are produced there. It used to be a prosperous fishing area in Jiaozhou Bay, but the industry has declined in recent years. Only in the spring are there still fishermen catching hairtail, while there are very few fishermen fishing in the autumn and winter. (10) Yinfu is located on the west coast of Jiaozhou Bay, about ten nautical miles from Qingdao. The island is surrounded by the sea on three sides, and people's livelihoods depend on fishing for about 70% of their income, in addition to agriculture accounting for 30-40%. The fishing season is entirely in the spring, and the whole year depends on this income. (11) Xuejiaqi, Huangdao, and Shuilingshan are in the same situation as Yin Island. (12) Zhucha Island is located southwest of Qingdao, about twenty nautical miles from Qingdao. The terrain is surrounded by the sea on all sides, and fishing is most prosperous in the spring season. The abundance of fish produced is no less than that of Shazikou.

Comparison of the Fishing Industry Then and Now: According to investigations, thirty years ago, there were more than 160 villages in the Qingdao area that were fishing villages, with about 20 villages in the Shazikou District, about 8-9 villages in the southern part of the Zhangcun District, about 20 villages in the Taitung District, about 30 villages in the Sifang District, about 10 villages in the western part of the Xianjiazhai District, and more than 70 villages in the entire Haixi area. Fishing households accounted for about half of the total number of households in each village. At present, apart from the Haixi area, which still relies on fishing as a secondary occupation, there are only about 30 households in the Shazikou District on the Haidong side, and very few people engaged in fishing in other areas. Compared to thirty years ago, the ratio is equal to one hundred to ten. According to investigations, the reasons for the decline of the fishing industry are nothing more than the following: 1. After Qingdao was opened as a commercial port, the standard of living increased daily, but the income from fishing could not be increased, resulting in many people abandoning the industry. 2. Fishermen adhered to old methods and did not know how to improve fishing gear and fishing methods. 3. Experiencing economic difficulties. 4. Pirates abounded. 5. The tax levies and donations were too heavy. 6. The government did not provide promotion or support, and the people were unable to improve. 7. Since the Third Year of the Republic, Japanese often intruded into our country's territorial waters to fish, resulting in reduced income for fishermen. Due to these various reasons, the fishing industry in Qingdao gradually declined and fell into a slump. (May 31st)

Jilin Province's Jingbo Lake

Organizational Plan for the Hydroelectric Power Company

First build a paper mill and sawmill, then gradually expand to

Make the Northeast an industrial zone that is completely electrified

Jilin Correspondence. Qian Zhaoxi, the former Military Governor of Rehe, and his associates initiated the organization of the Jingbo Lake Hydropower Company in September of last year, and the provincial government approved its establishment. Qian, together with electrical, civil engineering, and geological specialists, went to the site for a field survey on March 1st of this year, and the work has already been completed. It was decided to first trial-operate a paper mill and sawmill, organizing a limited company in accordance with the Company Law, with a total capital of 6 million national currency, divided into 300,000 shares. The head office will be located in Jilin, and branch offices may be established in Liaoning, Heilongjiang, and Rehe provinces as necessary. Once the capital is sufficient, operations will be expanded, with the aim of making the four northeastern provinces an industrial area that is completely electrified. The plan is quite ambitious, and many important figures in Jilin Province have also lent their names in support. An office has been set up in the provincial capital to prepare, and the company's articles of association, along with the investigation report, have been submitted to the provincial government for approval and filing, and the Construction and Agriculture & Mining Departments have been ordered to review any areas of the electrical business establishment and company articles of association that need to be supplemented or revised. Once the orders are followed, work can begin. This matter is extremely important for the development of the Northeast, so the investigation report is recorded as follows:

Location and Terrain: Jingbo Lake is located in Tiren Township, Ning'an County, Jilin Province, 110 miles southwest of the county seat, at 129 degrees east longitude and 44 degrees north latitude. It is surrounded by mountains, and the accumulated water forms a lake. The lake to the south is called Nantou Lake, and the lake to the north is called Beitou Lake. The two lakes together resemble an "S" shape. The lake surface is 80 miles long from north to south and 20 miles wide from east to west, varying between five and ten miles. The bottom of the lake is mountainous, with uneven elevations. The water depth ranges from 18 zhang to 8-9 zhang, with the water level being deeper in summer compared to spring by 1.3-1.4 chi. The lakeshore is covered with volcanic mountains and protruding rocks that rise dozens of zhang above the water surface. The source of the lake water is divided into two locations: The first originates from the south in Datoushi River, Songjiang River, Fangshengou River, and Xiaojiaji River; the second originates from the southwest, one from Emuxi County and one from Zhangguangcai Mountain Range and Dunhua South Mountain Range. These are the upper reaches of the Mudanjiang River. The outlet of the lake water is only the Zhangjialiangzi Waterfall at the north head of the lake, which is about 4-5 zhang wide. In winter, when the water dries up, it is only about one zhang wide. Below the waterfall is the Mudanjiang River, which is about 700 li long and flows into the Songhua River in Yilan.

Hydropower of the Waterfall: The Zhangjialiangzi Waterfall is the only channel for the lake water to flow into the Mudanjiang River. In winter, when the water dries up, the waterfall is only about one zhang wide, two zhang high, and one chi thick. In summer, it is more than ten zhang high, seven or eight zhang wide, and four or five chi thick. Below the waterfall is a round pool with a diameter of about thirty or forty zhang, surrounded by rocks that are more than ten zhang high. The locals say that the pool is about three li deep. The south of the waterfall is the lake water, the east is the rocky mountain, and the northwest are connected to the Shi Dianzi, a vast expanse of 200 li long and 20-30 li wide. This kind of place is extremely unsuitable for civil engineering work, and the natural waterfall is too large in summer and too small in winter. Even if reservoirs are built to store water for the winter, the water discharge project in the summer will be difficult. However, it is found that about eight miles east of the waterfall, the distance between the lake and the river is about five li in Sijitong Zhengou, where the lake water is twenty zhang higher than the river water. The mountain separating the lake and the river is about ten zhang high. By excavating a ditch through here to the south of the river, it is possible to obtain 500,000 to 800,000 horsepower according to the calculation of the drop flow and flow velocity. By utilizing this huge amount of hydropower, it is possible to obtain 370,000 to 600,000 kilowatts of electricity to supply the four northeastern provinces, with a surplus of 60-70%. The south side of Sijitong is along the lake shore, and the north side is mostly plains with good soil quality, which is conducive to construction. This kind of place is very suitable for an industrial area.

Resources: The land near Jingbo Lake is fertile, the population is sparse, and the benefits of mining, agriculture, land reclamation, fishing, animal husbandry, and hunting are limitless. Forty to fifty li from the south head of the lake is a huge forest that is vast and boundless, and people call it Fuhai. According to Japanese investigations, it is said that there are indeed 200 million tons of timber. If one million tons are harvested annually, it will take 200 years to continue harvesting without exhausting it. If electricity is used for processing and papermaking, it can not only supply Japan's domestic use, but also conquer the Republic of China, etc. Although the trees near the lake seem lush, they have been heavily harvested due to the convenience of lake water transportation, and there are no large forests. Gold sand is found in abundance in the mountains. I saw it in the lake and at the mouth of Chongchong River. According to the locals, the Lahei Mountain in the lake is rich in all kinds of metal ores. Investigations have revealed that gold mines have been reported in Ning'an County in Changshuigou, Liangshuiquanzi, Wuhulin, Huangnihe, Xiaoqingshan, Majiatang, and other places, but Wangqing County, Emuxi County, and Dongning County, which are within 200-300 li of the lake, are the richest gold-producing areas. Coal mines in Dongning County include Foyegou, Changdaoshan, Dawuxiaopo, Wuhulin, Bolih River, and Tangzi. Only Wuhulinzi was about to start mining, but it was stopped, and the rest have not been mined. The lake is rich in fish, with carp and crucian carp being the most abundant. However, the crucian carp is the most delicious and was a tribute during the Qing Dynasty. The mountains near the lake produce famous products like ginseng, astragalus, and mushrooms. The animals include tigers, leopards, bears, wolves, deer, sable, otters, foxes, and gray rats. The most important agricultural product is wheat, followed by millet, barley, soybeans, oats, and sorghum. The quality of wheat is good, and people say that the wheat produced in the eastern province is the best locally produced wheat.

Scenery and Climate: Jingbo Lake was called Wuhanhai in the Tang Dynasty and Biersheng Lake in the Qing Dynasty. Its current name is Jingbo Lake. The mountains are clear and the water is beautiful, and the scenery is excellent. In the lake are Da Gu Shan, Xiao Gu Shan, and Lao Guan Shan. Da Gu Shan is more than 700 chi above the water surface, towering in the lake. The confluence of Daoshi Mountain and Yuansai Mountain is recorded in the county chronicles as "Two Dragons Playing with Pearls". There is an ancient temple on it called the Sanqing Temple. Lao Guan Shan stands alone at the south end of the lake and is inhabited by countless waterfowl. The top is covered with white bird droppings, several inches thick, which from a distance almost looks like accumulated snow. There are also two small mountains standing side by side, like a door, named Zhenzhu Men. North of the door is an ancient city. In the first year of the Republic of China, a copper seal was discovered with the characters "Wuhanzhou Jiansanwang Dadudu" (General Military Governor of Wuhanzhou in charge of Three Kings). The east, north, and south sides of the city are steep cliffs bordering the lake, which people cannot climb. Only the southwest has a winding path that can be used to ascend the city. Traveling all over the lake fills people with pleasure. In summer and autumn, the flowers are red, the water is green, the fish are leaping, the birds are flying, the haze floats, and the sunlight covers the lake, like a natural painting. Some people say that the scenery here is the second best in the world. There is a monument under the waterfall with the inscription "China's First Waterfall", which shows the admiration of tourists. The climate is mild and similar to Changchun. The winters are harsh, with temperatures as low as -30 degrees Celsius. The waterfall does not freeze even in the severe winter.

Transportation: Starting from Sijitong at Jingbo Lake, it is 700 li southwest to Jilin Provincial City, 300 li to Dunhua, 360 li southeast to Yanji, 40 li northeast to Dongjingcheng Town, 110 li to Ning'an County, 160 li to Hailin Station on the Chinese Eastern Railway, 826 li northwest along the Chinese Eastern Railway to Harbin, and 530 li northeast to Suifenhe. Although the waterway through the Mudanjiang River is 700 li long and can reach Yilan, the downstream water flow is too rapid, and many large rocks are exposed on the surface, like stars in the sky, which the locals call "Full of Stars". It is extremely dangerous for ships to travel here. Only wooden rafts and small boats transport garlic, wild vegetables, etc. and sell them together with the boats when they reach Yilan, never returning because it is very difficult to go upstream. Taking the Chinese Eastern Railway from Harbin to the east for 666 li to Hailin Station, there is a long-distance bus to Ning'an County, 50 li, which can be reached in about an hour. Traveling another 70 li south to Dongjingcheng can also be reached by bus in about three hours in winter. It is necessary to take a four-wheeled cart from Dongjingcheng to Sijitong, 40 li. Travel in the summer is slightly difficult. Miscellaneous records state that the farmers living near Jingbo Lake often saw Russians coming here to investigate before the first year of the Republic of China. After the first year of the Republic of China, people from England, France, and the United States also came to ask questions. However, the Japanese have been coming since the seventh year of the Republic of China until the tenth year. During these four years, four people lived here to survey every spring, summer, autumn, and winter. Each season, a shift was replaced, and they continued to come and go. They did not come in the eleventh year of the Republic of China. They investigated every aspect of the soil quality, water volume, topography, and climate in great detail. The domestic people have not seen a single person come here to investigate. Now, seeing them, I am very happy and follow them around all day, guiding them to where the watermarks were set up, where the ice was dug to measure the water, and where the soil was dug and taken away, as if counting family treasures, and speaking without reservation. Some patriotic comrades in the academic community have notebooks with records that they give as gifts, and their enthusiasm and support are moving, further strengthening our original aspirations.

Important News Two

Zhejiang Provincial Government's Relief for the Silk Industry

All new electric looms are exempt from taxes.

Zhejiang is China's southeastern sericulture region, and silk and satin have always been its major products. However, since recent years, the industry has declined indescribably. The biggest reason is that the designs are outdated and there is no innovation, and most of the weaving is done by wooden looms, resulting in products that are dull and lackluster, unable to compete with foreign goods. Zhang, the chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, decided to promote and relieve the silk industry, and decided that if people can use the latest European and American electric weaving machines to set up factories, they can be exempt from taxes after submitting an application to the Department of Construction and being approved by personnel sent for inspection. A proposal has been drawn up and submitted to the 311th meeting of the Provincial Government Committee for resolution and approval. The Provincial Government has now instructed the Department of Construction to forward the order to the counties, instructing their subordinate silk industries to be informed.

The Passage of the Tongshen Steamer Back to Harbin

The ship stayed in Hulin for more than a year due to avoiding the Russian chaos.

The return to Harbin under orders was quite thrilling along the way.

Harbin Correspondence. The Tongshen steamer, which had been moored in Hulin to avoid the Russian incident last year, only set sail back on May 18th of this year. The crew experienced many hardships along the way, and the crew returned to their homeland as if after a lifetime. It returned to Harbin Port at 4 pm on the 28th, and docked at the Toutiao Street pier at 9 am on the 29th to unload cargo. After unloading, it berthed on the north bank of the river. It is scheduled to enter the dock for repairs in a day or two and will resume sailing to Hulin on June 14th. According to Zhao Zi'an, the first mate of the ship, the passage of the ship back was as follows:

"Our ship was docked in mid-June of last year when the Russian incident was about to change. I was afraid that it would be dangerous to sail back, and there would be no good outcome, so I docked on our shore in Hulin. Although I could not avoid the alarm of war during the emergency period of the Sino-Russian war, I did not see any facts. In April of this year, I planned to return, and I fired up the engine three times, but I stopped because I was worried about the danger. On May 2nd, the telegraph line between Hulin and Tongjiang was repaired, so I sent a telegram to the headquarters (Navigation Bureau) asking for instructions. On the 5th, I received a reply ordering me to sail back to the port as soon as possible. I telegraphed back that the river channel was dangerous and could not be guaranteed to be free from accidents. Once sailing, the lives and property of the entire ship would have no protection. How should the headquarters handle it? Please give instructions. Then I received a reply saying that the Ussuri and Heilong Rivers are border rivers of the country, and China has its own navigation rights. Now, I am ordered by the National Government to order the ship to return as soon as possible, and all employees will be rewarded generously. The Sino-Russian conference will be held soon, and all other matters need not be considered. After receiving the telegram, I gathered the entire ship's machinists, helmsmen, sailors, etc. and told them the meaning of the telegram. All the employees said that they would only follow the first mate's orders, so I decided to set sail on the 18th. At 6 am, I ordered the engineer to sound the whistle three times according to the ship's regulations and solemnly hung the national flag and the ship emblem. At that time, all the people in Hulin City were alarmed. From the county magistrate to the women and children, many people went to the river to see us off. Most people thought I was nosy, thinking that it was still impossible to set sail. Now that I have set sail, I am blowing the whistle and hanging the flag to alarm the Russian soldiers on the opposite bank. I am afraid that if they do not fire cannons to block the way at this time, it will be difficult to escape the danger. I didn't think so, because I know that I am a Chinese man and woman, I am a Chinese captain, and my ship is sailing in the Sino-Russian border river with justice and righteousness, so what do I have to fear? However, to prevent any accidents, I secretly ordered the engineer to release full horsepower to move forward. When the ship left the Hulin shore, I still saw the crowd shaking their heads and sighing. From Hulin to Tongjiang, we passed through four Russian checkpoints, namely (1) Kayilin, (2) Qiaobozi, (3) Wangbabozi, and (4) Haiqing Fishing Ground. All of the above four checkpoints were heavily guarded by Russian troops. The main stream of the river had been cut down by our side during the anti-Russian campaign last year, so we had to sail close to the Russian bank. Although I knew it was dangerous, there was no other way. At 8 am, the first checkpoint, which was 20 li from Hulin, was on the opposite bank of our land. The office of the Northeast Navigation Bureau was originally located here. The director of the office, Mr. Tang, heard that our ship was sailing, so he hired a special person to watch the river bank to see the Russian side's movements, intending to warn us in case of an accident. Our ship was less than a li away from our shore, and the army went to the river bank in surprise to see the ship sailing, as if they were very surprised, but our ship took the opportunity to accelerate and the fate of the entire ship was entrusted to the engine and the waves. At about 9 am, we passed the second checkpoint, Qiaobozi. The chief pilot Yao Xing (i.e., the chief helmsman) pointed to the black shadow of the mountain in front of us and told us to pay attention. I looked at it with binoculars and saw that the mountains were covered with Russian cavalry soldiers aiming their guns at our ship. I thought that I would not be lucky, so I ordered all the employees on the ship to lie down on the deck, and the helm house was also blocked with armor. This kind of armor was prepared by me in Hulin to prevent accidents on the way. At this time, I took the opportunity to use it. I stood alone in the helm house to direct the engineer to release full horsepower to sail. The ship was sailing at a very high speed, almost unknown how many li per hour. As soon as we passed the side of the mountain, the Russian cavalry rushed down from the mountain and scattered to the riverside. Our ship had already sailed out two li at an extremely fast speed. Looking back at the Russian soldiers, they seemed quite disappointed, shouldered their guns, tightened their reins, and turned their horses away. At about 11 am, we passed the third checkpoint, "Wang Yiba Zi". Looking from afar, the Russian soldiers were in and out of the Russian camp, seeming very confused and pointing at our ship and talking to each other. Our ship crossed before they could decide, and stopped at Tuanshanzi, which belongs to Hulin, that night. The distance was 200 li from Hulin. On the morning of the 19th, we set off again. There were no obstacles along the way. We arrived safely in Raohe in the afternoon and anchored for the night. I got off the ship and told the people from all walks of life in Hulin via long-distance telephone. The other side was very happy for us. On the morning of the 20th, we set off again. The chief pilot Yao Xing suddenly fell ill, probably due to months of worry and hard work, but he still tried his best to support and serve. At 4 pm, we passed the Haiqing Fishing Ground, which was originally our land, but the Russians stationed heavy troops on the opposite bank and called it the fourth checkpoint. Before the Sino-Russian war, our ships often suffered attacks when sailing through this place, and merchants regarded it as a place of fear. We did not dare to celebrate after passing three checkpoints, so we finally determined our fate after passing this place. The ship was sailing closer when we suddenly saw dozens of Russian soldiers rushing out of the barracks and aiming their guns at our ship. I quickly assisted the chief pilot in drumming the wheel to drive the ship. The area is the intersection of the Ussuri and Heilong Rivers, connecting the Ussuri and Heilong Rivers with a river branch called Tongjiangzi, which is hundreds of li long. The harbor fork is winding and not easy to travel. Our merchant ships must pass through this fork when traveling to the Ussuri River. If we sail into this river, it will not be visible to the Russian checkpoint. Therefore, our ship tried its best to turn the rudder and rushed into Tongjiangzi. The Russian soldiers lost their target and stopped shooting. Just as my soul was about to settle down, I encountered an accident. Our ship was moving forward in the bushes when I saw black smoke rising in the air, gathering in the air, as if there were ships sailing ahead. Russian ships, except for warships, do not use coal. In other words, it can be proved by the black smoke that the ship in front was undoubtedly a Russian warship. However, our ship was like an arrow on the string and had to be fired, so we still tried our best to sail forward. It was not until a dozen or so li away that we knew that the black smoke was gathering at the intersection of the Heilong and Ussuri Rivers, which was still far away from our route. Therefore, the hearts of the crew were relieved. On the evening of the 21st, it was raining heavily and the river surface was dark and invisible. I was in charge of the ship and moved forward in the dark. There was no pier to dock at, so I had to desperately sail forward. The rain became heavier and heavier at midnight. In order to protect the lives of the entire ship, I was standing on the upper deck, looking ahead, when I suddenly saw two points of light about a li ahead of our ship moving very fast. Our ship tried its best to chase after them. At 1 am on the 22nd, we had already caught up, because the two points of light had stopped moving in the middle of the river. Our ship sailed past, and we almost fainted in shock, because the two points of light were none other than the mast lights of two huge Russian warships. Their soldiers came out to inspect as our ship passed, and fortunately they did not raise their anchors. Our ship sailed out dozens of li, and because it was dark, we could not move forward, so we stopped the ship in the river. We set sail again at 3 am on the 22nd and arrived at Chendeli at 9 am. I went ashore and asked the Tongjiang Navigation Bureau by telephone whether there were any Russian ships outside the river mouth. According to them, three ships had been berthed a few days ago, but they had already left, and the mines had been cleared, so it was safe to sail. At 8 pm that afternoon, we passed the Russian shore of Xuergu. At 7 pm, we arrived at the Sanjiang Estuary, and at 7:30 pm, we returned to Tongjiang. At that time, the Suzhou ship was firing up the engine, waiting to see how our ship would test the waters before deciding on a plan. After our ship arrived, the Suzhou ship sailed to Heihe at 7 am on the 23rd. In short, I was so frightened along the way back from Hulin that I had never experienced it in my 20 years of life on the river. Fortunately, we sailed back safely and reported to the public and private sectors without any blame." (30th)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

Summary of the First District Affairs Meeting: The first district of this county held its ninth district affairs meeting yesterday (the 4th). The following is a summary of the important matters: (1) Citizen Oath Registration: The county magistrate will complete the process by the end of June. The township heads and town chiefs shall follow the rules and complete the process on schedule and report it. (2) Personnel Registration: Following the order to strictly urge registration, the district office will issue a notice and send various forms to the township heads and town chiefs to actively promote the registration and report it to the district office. (3) Land Registration: The number of registrations is still very small. The provincial order's deadline is approaching, and the township heads and town chiefs should promote and urge business owners to come to the office to register. (4) Implementing Price Stabilization: It will be implemented next month. The district office will order the township police to investigate extremely poor households, create a register, and report it. The township heads and town chiefs will then be issued a letter to investigate one by one and submit it to the office for review at the district affairs meeting, and then post it in sections to ensure fairness. (5) Village System Expenses for the 17th Year: The former street leaders have been urging for subsidies. The originally planned method was submitted to the county magistrate and then to the district affairs meeting for discussion and approval for submission. It was found that the former street leaders had advanced funds for public affairs and should be compensated. However, the amount of village system expenses is not large. It is decided to subsidize each street ten yuan, and the remaining balance will be waived to conclude the matter, and reported to the county government for record. (6) Stipulating that each township and town recruit thirty-five sanitation workers to provide segmented services during the summer hygiene period, and instructing the four sub-stations to supervise. (7) It is decided to administer vaccinations starting from June 20th. (8) According to the county magistrate's order, eliminate rice stem borer eggs, which should be handled under the supervision of the township heads and town chiefs, and reported for further submission.

Public Security Bureau Begins Moving to New Residence: Because the county urgently needs to establish a county court, it was determined that the Public Security Bureau's building would be the court's address. The Public Security Bureau is moving to the front of Puzhao Temple to conduct business. The repair work in front of Puzhao Temple has been completed. The first sub-station attached to the Public Security Bureau was ordered to move to the new office yesterday (the 4th) to conduct business. The general bureau will begin moving tomorrow.

Suzhou

Re-Appointment of Prison Wardens: Lin, the president of the Jiangsu Higher Court, previously appointed Xu Ji, the prison warden of Yizheng County, but due to certain matters, he was unable to take office. Therefore, on (the 3rd), he re-appointed Mei Shuchen, the warden of Qidong County Detention Center, to fill the position. The vacancy in Qidong was filled by Wang Kaiji as an agent. Also, Cheng Zhenlin, the prison warden of Guanyun County, resigned due to certain matters. The resignation was approved, and Xiang Jiahuang was appointed to fill the vacancy.

Summary of Public Security Bureau Meeting: The County Public Security Bureau held its second bureau affairs meeting yesterday (the 4th), chaired by Secretary Huang. The following is a summary of the resolutions: Currently, approximately one thousand wounded armed comrades have been transported from the front lines. It is proposed to organize fifteen rear hospitals in Suzhou. In the future, when encountering inquiries from officers and soldiers of the hospital, the police at each post must answer peacefully and pay attention to etiquette to show respect. The resolution was approved.

Over Four Hundred Wounded Soldiers Pass Through: Military officers Zhou and Zhang of the Ministry of Military Affairs escorted over four hundred wounded soldiers from the capital to Hangzhou for treatment yesterday (the 4th).

Actively Widening Guanqian Street: The county government held a county administration meeting yesterday and resolved that (1) houses on Guanqian Street that have not been acquired must be demolished by July 10th, and all road works must be completed by September. (2) The Public Security Bureau requested that the tea police donations be collected, transferred, and sent to the finance bureau for unified expenditure. The resolution was retained.

Gangster Activity Rises: Large gangs of lake bandits have been repeatedly defeated by military and police forces and scattered in various locations. Therefore, the Taihu Lake and Yangcheng Lake areas have been relatively peaceful for only a little over a month. However, it is known that two gangs from Henan and Haizhou combined in Zhejiang a few days ago and roamed to Zhouzhuang and Jinze, intending to disturb the area. The Taibao Ashu gang in Pudong also took the opportunity to become active and gathered in the vicinity of Qianwei Town in Jinshan County a few days ago, with a total of three hundred bandits secretly meeting to plot harm to the local area. Qian, the county magistrate of the county, learned of the news through intelligence reports and immediately telegraphed the Songhu Garrison Headquarters and the first district of Minhang Water Public Security to request that a team be sent immediately to suppress the bandits in order to reassure the people and avoid harm to the local area.

Wujiang

County Executive and Supervisory Committee Members Elected: The ninth county-wide representative assembly of this county was held on May 30th. The opening ceremony was held on the 30th, the meeting was held on the 31st, and the election was held on June 1st. Xu Yinshi, Zhu Yunji, Wu Yuefu, Lu Jianfei, Mao Xiaocen, and Zhang Beihu have been elected as candidates for the executive committee, and Qian Xigu, Yang Zichun, Zhu Zhenxiao, Mei Fulin, etc. have been elected as members of the supervisory committee. The list was submitted to the province for selection yesterday.

New County Magistrate Takes Office: The newly appointed County Magistrate Wu Jia arrived in the county on the afternoon of the 2nd of this month to take office. It is said that there will be many changes in the personnel of the county government's various sections this time, but they have not yet been announced. It is generally believed that Wu Hongyi, the head of the first section, will remain unchanged, and the entire secretariat may be reorganized.

Robbery Occurs in Meili Village: A robbery occurred at the home of farmer Hu Jinlong in Meili Village outside the west gate of this city the night before last, resulting in a loss of several hundred yuan.

Qingpu

Elementary School Teacher Strangles His Wife: Huang Yixin, an elementary school teacher in Huangdu Town in this county, married Jin Heting's daughter from the same town in 1920. They had one son and two daughters. Jin's mother's family was considered relatively well-off. After her father passed away, she often asked her mother for money for her husband to squander. Recently, it was discovered that his wife had received a savings of five hundred yuan, so he repeatedly threatened her to demand money. Because of his recklessness, Jin kindly advised him, but he was always beaten. Jin was a weak woman deeply influenced by old etiquette, so she swallowed her tears and washed her face with tears. Because he was unable to get what he wanted, Huang used extremely cruel methods to tie up Jin in the front room and beat her to death with a door bolt and other objects. By the next day, neighbors did not see Jin and became suspicious. They pushed straight in and saw Jin's body lying across the room, covered in bruises. Her mother, who was over sixty years old, rushed to the scene after hearing the news and was heartbroken. The incident has been reported to the county for investigation, and the murderer has been detained for investigation.

Burning Opium and Assigning Personnel to Monitor: The county government of this county held a ceremony to burn opium and opium paraphernalia on June 3rd. Chen Zhongda, the county magistrate of Jiading, was specially assigned by the Department of Civil Affairs to Qingpu to supervise the event. The anti-drug movement conference was held in the morning, and the burning ceremony was held in front of the Zhongshan Hall of the county government in the afternoon. It is reported that a total of more than seventy taels of opium and more than two hundred sets of opium paraphernalia were burned.

Welcoming and Arresting a Female Bandit for Trial: The Qingpu Water Public Security Team learned that when a bandit den was destroyed in Zhuangjiazhai, Nanhui County, Zhu Jizhou, who was abducted from Chonggu, was rescued on the spot, and the female bandit Zhuang Wu was captured. Deng Zi requested that the county government of the county prepare a document and order the police to welcome and arrest the female bandit and bring her back for trial.

Qinghu Section Culvert Bidding: The Qinghu section of the Shuhu Road in this county, except for the section of the airfield road, which was hindered due to military scope, has been suspended. The other sections have been completed in sequence. In order to facilitate agricultural work, the Construction Bureau is now bidding for the construction of fifty culverts and waterways in the entire section, which is scheduled to open on June 4th at 11:00 am. As for the airfield route, it is impossible to change it, and the situation has been reported to the provincial authorities to maintain the original route.

Wuxi

Large Batch of Red Pills Transported to Wuxi Seized: Guo Enbo, a native of Shandong, used to be a railway police officer at a certain station on the Jinghu Railway. He was recently dismissed due to certain matters. Recently, he has been engaged in selling red pills. Yesterday, Guo carried 35,000 red pills from Shanghai to Wuxi, intending to sell them. When the train arrived at Zhoujing Lane at 7:30 pm, he got off. Zhang Yutian (said to be surnamed Yang from Shandong) in a yellow uniform spotted him and immediately followed him. He followed Guo to the Wudong First Hotel on the road and threatened him in every possible way. As a result, all the red pills he was carrying were seized. Guo Enbo did not dare to speak out and left dejectedly.

Panic Over the Future of People's Food Supply: Since the beginning of spring in Wuxi, the price of rice has gradually risen and cannot be curbed. Although the government has advised rice merchants to consider the people's food supply, limit rice prices, and prohibit exports, the speakers are earnest and the listeners are indifferent. Now that summer has arrived, rice merchants are again using the pretext that the supply is scarce due to the transition period and gradually raising the price of rice. As of yesterday, the market price of white rice had risen to 17.2 yuan per dan and is likely to continue to rise. The common people who depend on grain are greatly alarmed.

Daytime Robbery Case in Jihuayuan Lane: Li Yonglian, also known as Ronglin, a teacher at the Zhenyi Silk Factory outside the South Gate, is responsible for teaching the children of the factory workers and lives in the factory's Jihuayuan Lane workshop. Around 2:00 pm the day before yesterday, four robbers wearing white short shirts and pants and undershirts, carrying knives and iron rulers, arrived at Li's house one after another. One person stayed outside to keep watch, and the other three entered to rob. First, they tied up Li's sister, Ye Li, with a rope and rubbed her lips with a knife, shouting, "If you make a sound, I'll cut you!" Ye was too frightened to make a sound. Li's wife and daughter happened to be at the factory, so the robbers went upstairs and directly entered Yonglian's room to search. After about forty minutes, they took the loot and left with the lookout, passing the small wooden bridge and heading towards Baoshan Temple. Afterwards, Ye shouted loudly and told the neighbors. Yonglian checked the lost items, which included fifty yuan in silver dollars, one hundred and fifty yuan in banknotes, gold hairpins, gold bracelets, and single-layer clothing, bedding, etc., worth more than three hundred yuan in total. He immediately reported the incident to the Public Security Sub-Bureau of the camp, which forwarded it to the authorities for investigation. In the evening, Luo Xiaoda, a member of the Third Sub-Bureau, arrested a suspect named Li Huzi in front of Baoshan Temple, but he was found to be unrelated and was released on bail.

Summary of Rural Robbery Cases: Xu Yongkang, who lives in the vicinity of Dongfeng, Yangming Township, Third District, has been doing business in Shanghai. There are few people living at home. The night before last, many robbers carrying guns and flashlights broke into the house and searched everywhere for about an hour before taking the loot out. After checking, it was found that a total of more than two hundred yuan was lost. Yesterday, Yongkang sent a letter to the county reporting the incident and requesting investigation. Also, at 1:00 am the night before last, more than ten robbers in Youdu Village, Jingyun City, blatantly knocked on the door of Xu Shougen. Several other robbers were guarding the back door of Xu's house. The back door had been broken. The robbers poured in. Xu Shougen's son hurriedly held a gong and climbed onto the roof, banging loudly to alarm the neighbors, who rushed to the rescue. The robbers then dispersed and fled.

Court Interrogation Record of a False Robbery Report Case: Cao Haochu, the accountant of the Luhangxing Foundry in Tonghui Bridge, received a total of 400 yuan in silver dollars and banknotes from Chen Zufu in Qingyang Town on the 29th of last month. The next day, he took a boat back to Wuxi. Not long after arriving at the port, he went to the Sixth Public Security Sub-Bureau to report that he had been robbed by two robbers near Liangba who opened fire and stole all 400 yuan he had collected. The sub-bureau found many suspicious points in his statement. In addition to investigating the case, it prepared a document and sent him to the County Public Security Bureau, which forwarded him to the County Government. Zhou Zitun, the trial judge, opened the court for interrogation yesterday. According to Cao Haochu's confession, he held the bag of money when the boat arrived at the dock, but the crowd was crowded and he accidentally let go of it. Suddenly, it was stolen. He was extremely anxious at the time and intended to commit suicide by jumping into the river. Then he thought that the stolen money was a mistake, and it was useless to die. However, he was mentally confused and after much thought, he falsely reported a robbery in the hope of concealing the matter. However, his relationship with the factory owner was very good, and he could not bear to cause him losses. Now, he had no choice but to sell his property to repay the debt. He knew that the false report of the robbery was inappropriate and requested leniency. Zhou Jun verified the confession and determined that his statement was factual. He ordered him to provide a guarantor to leave and handle the matter, pending investigation and verification.

Changzhou

First Day of Budget Meeting: The Wuyi County Government convened various agencies at 4:00 pm on the 3rd to hold a local budget meeting to discuss proposals: (1) Zhuang Zhongxi, Director of the Construction Bureau, proposed that the administrative income of each agency be listed and submitted to the Finance Bureau. The resolution was passed. (2) Xu Wenjun of the County Rectification Committee proposed that the reduction be discussed first and then the increase. The resolution was passed. (3) He also proposed that the police team's firearms expenses should be reduced. The resolution was passed and the original plan of 5,000 yuan was retained. (4) County Magistrate Wu proposed that due to the urgent time, the budget meeting be changed to 9:00 am on the 4th for a review meeting and 1:00 pm for a continuation of the budget meeting. The resolution was passed. (5) The results of the election of reviewers were Yang Changyou, Xu Wenjun, Min Yicheng, Qian Ziwei, and Huang Lemin. They were elected and then adjourned.

Kidnapping Case Near Yuncun: The home of farmer Wang Jinzhao in Changxicun near Yuncun, Wuyi County, was robbed by bandits the night before last. The victim was tied up and threatened with guns. Then, they searched and looted the property. When they left, they tied Wang Jinzhao and took him away by boat at Dahekou, heading towards Yixing. After the incident, Lei Chou, the director of the eighth public security sub-bureau in charge, went to pursue the bandits but failed to find them. He surveyed the area for a week and reported the case to the Public Security Bureau on the 3rd, requesting investigation.

Nantong

All Circles Thoroughly Investigate Opium Trafficking Case: The opium trafficking case in Tongyi has been widely publicized. For days, there have been rumors of opium traffickers bribing local authorities. On the 3rd, all circles held a meeting at the county government and unanimously advocated a thorough investigation. The Press Federation held a special meeting at 7:00 pm to discuss the matter and decided that each newspaper should report as much as possible on the news of the opium trafficking case.

Military and Police Teams Launch Large-Scale Bandit Suppression: Bandits have been harassing the border area between Nantong, Rugao, and Haimen counties in Jiangbei. Recently, the wheat harvest has been completed and obstacles have been removed. The national army, provincial police team, and local security corps stationed in the area have jointly formed a bandit suppression team to launch a large-scale encirclement and suppression of the bandits. On the one hand, they are taking over the work of clearing the countryside and searching for lurking bandits. All telephone exchanges in the bandit area have been destroyed. The military and police have set up a telecommunications traffic team to work with the army. On the other hand, the Jiangbei Bandit Suppression Headquarters has requested the provincial government to allocate military shortwave wireless radios for use.

Police Team Repels Bandit Boat: More than ten bandit boats suddenly arrived at the Yingfang Port in Tongyi. Fifty bandits carrying weapons landed ashore, hoping to rob. The Pingchao police team stationed there intercepted them, and the bandits boarded the boat and retreated. Three bandits were captured and sent to the county government for interrogation.

Jiangyin

Ambiguous Departure of Sub-Bureau Chief: Peng Ze (Zijie Shi), the chief of the North Wai Public Security First Sub-Bureau, was appointed after the new bureau chief Li Zong took office. Less than a month after his appointment, Mao Mujun, the district chief of the Second District of the Water Public Security Team, came to Cheng from Wuxi on the Jing'an warship on the 3rd and contacted County Magistrate Li. Then, he took Peng Ze to Wuxi. The sub-bureau affairs were handled by Cui Siping, the section chief of the Third Section of the Public Security Bureau. It is said that Peng had uncleared matters when he was the captain of the sixth team in the Second District of the Water Police. Mao and Peng decided to take a warship to Wuxi on the morning of the 4th. They were extremely secretive to the outside world, only saying that Peng's father was critically ill in Suzhou and had asked for a few days' leave. The official denied and refused to announce other reasons.

Court Interrogation of Chen Songshan's Dereliction of Duty Case: Chen Songshan, the head of the Deshun Township Security Corps, was accused by Shi Xilin of killing his brother Shi Daguan and moving the body. The case of dereliction of duty was transmitted to a thousand witnesses for interrogation by Judge Yang on the evening of yesterday (the 3rd). Shi Xilin and his mother Yao both testified that after Daguan was detained, he entrusted Wang Dayi, Chen Guanlin, and Cai Rujin to provide a guarantee of eight yuan in bureau fees, but he was still not released. He suddenly hanged himself and died. He also had no illness. Therefore, they suspected whether he was beaten to death or hanged to death, which was difficult to determine. The judge said that he had witnessed the autopsy and confirmed that the deceased had indeed hanged himself. If it was clearly stated that he was beaten to death, he would have to provide a counterclaim guarantee in accordance with the law and submit it to the High Court for review and verification in order to make it clear. Shi Xilin replied that he only suspected that he was beaten to death and it was difficult to guess. The judge then interrogated the guarantors Wang Dayi and others. They testified that they went to guarantee Daguan twice but he was not released. The third time they went to guarantee, Commander Chen agreed but did not release him, and they did not know about the rest of the matter. Chen Songshan testified that if he had beaten Shi Daguan to death, he would be willing to be shot and requested a review. After the interrogation, Chen Songshan was released on bail pending further investigation and interrogation, and the others were ordered to return. The court was then adjourned.

Body Standing Upright in the River: A male corpse was suddenly found in the small river behind Bu Jiacun, Sixth Bao, Changshou Township, yesterday morning. The corpse was about twenty years old and looked like a businessman. The body was standing upright in the river, not falling down, which was quite strange. The Security Corps called the county government, and Judge Yang was sent to the countryside to conduct an autopsy this morning.

Revenge for Hatred by Opium Traffickers: Wen Renfu, who used to be an inspector in Zhang Pinquan's Public Security Bureau when he was the bureau chief in the downtown area of Zhongjie, is now a detective in the Nantong Water Public Security Team. On the evening of the 2nd, Zhang Zongsi, an opium trafficker, and his brother suddenly asked Wen for 250 yuan in owed money, saying that it was handled by Lu Juqiu and there was a written record as evidence. Wen then twisted Zhang Zongsi and others to the Public Security Bureau, saying that Zhang and others were in the form of kidnapping. He used to be a public official, but now he has retired. Suddenly, he came to retaliate against the working personnel. Wouldn't it be dangerous? Then, Huang Jinbiao and others persuaded him to leave. Wen Renfu formally filed a lawsuit yesterday.

Danyang

Robbery and Injury in Yetian Village: More than twenty bandits suddenly broke into the home of farmer Cai Cong in Yetian Village, south of Shicheng, the night before last, and looted extensively. They also robbed the homes of nearby Cai Luo Xiao. After checking, the total loss was estimated to be about 200 yuan in silver dollars and jewelry. Cai Luo Xiao's mother was seriously injured and the case has been reported for investigation.

Teacher Causes Trouble at Sports Meet: The Danyang Experimental Girls' Elementary School held a sports meet in the park yesterday. A female student was running a race with eggs when Xiao Long, a nephew of the bystander Shen Lao Er, knocked the egg to the ground. Teacher Wu became furious and kicked Xiao Long severely, causing him to fall to the ground injured. The audience was outraged and questioned him. Xiao Long's mother also rushed to the scene after hearing the news and twisted the teacher to the Public Security Bureau. Later, Wu, the teacher, was instructed by the mediator to bear the medical expenses, and the matter was resolved peacefully.

Zhenjiang

Jiangsu Provincial Government's Method of Hiring: Since the reorganization of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, no less than two thousand people have been introduced from all parties as county magistrates and public security bureau chiefs. The congestion in the official career is alarming. The provincial government now intends to adopt a selection method. Roughly, each member of the concurrent office will conduct a detailed review first. Those who pass the review will number about seventy people. It is intended to fill out the review qualification form in accordance with the county magistrate's appointment regulations, together with supporting documents, and first hold a general conversation with the introducers, and then have each member talk separately to determine whether they are qualified or not. At the same time, the person introduced by the member and qualified after his review must be fully responsible by the member. As for those who have passed the selection, before being appointed, they will be given considerable work as a test. If the results are excellent, they will be formally appointed. This method is still in the experimental stage. Recently, the provincial government has appointed about twenty county magistrates. The date of their arrival in office varies from one month to two months. Among these twenty people, two have now been accused and the provincial government has sent people to investigate secretly. It is now heard that the central government has approved the county magistrate examination and it can be held in June or July. The selection method may need to be changed in the future.

Villagers in Eastern Town Burn Bandits to Death: In the Guanshan Temple area of Zhenjiang East Town, bandits have been gathering and looting in recent days, and there have been cases of kidnapping and burning. The villagers are anxious and sleepless, hating the bandits to the core. The day before yesterday, hundreds of people gathered and searched for bandits everywhere. They searched and captured one bandit each in Zongzhang Lane, Shiqiao Tou, and Bei Wang Lane, and seven bandits in Hou Li and other places, for a total of ten. After discussion, it was decided to burn the ten bandits together to warn the future and vent their hatred for the harassment.

Results of the National Arts Branch Examination Announced: The Jiangsu Provincial National Arts Branch recruited the second class of normal school students the day before yesterday. A total of forty-five people recommended by various public security agencies were present. The examination committee of the branch has now evaluated the results and posted the list of those who have been admitted and those who have been rejected. It has also sent a telegram urging the county governments and water police teams that have not yet recommended to do so by the deadline. The list of the names of the members admitted by the branch is as follows: (31 regularly admitted members) Wan Bin, Wan Liang, Wu Xueyi, Gao Pengxian, Xu Jing, Wang Yu bao, Chang Zhao chun, Chen Jiaju, Shen Jin, Liang Yunpeng, Diao Yaozong, Ren Zhongmei, Yao Dong, Li Hongsheng, Weng Jifu, Ye Mao, Hao Zhihua, Yang Zichun, Zhu Shiwen, Huang Hongsheng, Cheng Yuelou, Yang Yunshan, Ding Fengchi, Duan Zongrui, Tu Lunzhan, Ma Chi, Yan Zhenhua, Wang Wei, Xu Tianyun, Qin Shihai, Zhang Ruyu (alternates) Wang Hongjia

Yangzhou

Segmented Protection for Navigation: Because there have been cases of bandits looting boats along the canal, a meeting was previously held to discuss escort measures. On the 2nd, the Public Security Bureau, the Police Team, and the Sixth District of the Water Public Security jointly decided on the following segmented protection measures: (1) From Yangzi Bridge to Wantou, the Public Security Fourth Sub-station will be responsible. From Wantou to Shaobo, the Police Team will be responsible. From Shaobo to Lujin, the Eighth Sub-Bureau will be responsible. From Lujin to Gaoyou, the Sixth District will be responsible.

Telegram Reporting Clash Between Camp Soldiers and Security Corps: Zhang Jia Rui, the Huaiyun Envoy, and Tang Ken, the Director of the Huainan Smuggling Suppression Camp Bureau, reported yesterday (the 2nd) the details of the clash between the soldiers of the Second Battalion of the Infantry Camp for Smuggling Suppression stationed in Haimen and the local Security Corps, according to a telegram from the Haimen County Government. In addition to reporting directly to the Department of Civil Affairs and the Department of Military Affairs and Smuggling Suppression, they requested review.

Tobacco Merchants Oppose the Director of the Tax Collection Office: Yangzhou tobacco merchants held a meeting at the Guangye Public Office on the 3rd to discuss dealing with Wu Chida, the Director of the Tobacco License Tax Collection Office, and decided on (1) not to resist taxes, (2) not to recognize Wu personally, and (3) not to stop until Wu is removed. It is heard that the reason is that Wu, who also serves as the head of the Public Security Bureau's registration of female singers, has abused his power to falsely accuse Dong and two unrelated merchants of resisting taxes and has asked the Public Security Bureau to arrest them. It is now heard that Wu will continue to serve, so they are trying to resist.

Jiaxing

River Works Completed, Boat Traffic Resumes as Normal: Since the opening of the Tongde Line from Puyuan Town to Chang'an Station on the Huhangyong Line, travel has been convenient. The towns of Shimen and Tongxiang that it passes through are also major towns in Hezhong. Last autumn, boat traffic was suspended due to the dam break in the canal for dredging, causing hardship for passengers. Now that the river works have been completed, boat traffic has resumed as normal since the 20th of last month, which is convenient at a time when silkworm cocoons are on the market.

Huzhou

Xu Jinian Escapes from Two Kidnapping Attempts: Xu Jinian (also known as Si Bao Xiang) of Da Sizha west of Xucang Bridge in Huzhou has a considerable fortune and has long been coveted by bandits. Because Xu is good at defending himself, wears tattered clothes, and often pretends to be a coolie, the bandits have no way to start. On the 31st of last month, Xu went to Xucang Bridge to shop and was about two miles away from Zha on his way home when he encountered a bandit wearing a yuan yu gauze long gown. The bandit took out a pistol from his sleeve and forbade Xu from making a sound or shouting, asking if he was the Si Bao boss. Xu replied that he was not and that his surname was Yang. Three other bandits twisted Xu to the woods and searched him all over, robbing him of one silver dollar, six small silver coins, more than forty copper coins, three yellow croaker fish, more than a catty of pork, and several packets of tea snacks. Xu Jinian escaped home. Unexpectedly, on the evening of the same day, more than ten bandits armed with guns broke through the wall and entered. Xu could not avoid being dragged away by the bandits, who said, "Is your fourth boss at home?" Xu hurriedly said he was at Xucang Bridge. The bandits let go of Xu and searched everywhere upstairs, finding nothing and robbing all the clothes and other items, resulting in a loss of more than 300 yuan. Although Xu encountered bandits twice in one day, he was lucky to escape both times due to his quick wit.

Bandits Threaten Monks: At Hongxi Temple in Jinjia Lane, West Gate of this city, at about 3:00 pm the day before yesterday, a bandit wearing short clothes suddenly arrived. The abbot Liankui happened to be out attending religious services, leaving only a seven-year-old novice monk in the temple. The bandit asked where the abbot was, and the novice monk replied that he had gone out to attend religious services. The bandit left a letter asking to borrow 1,400 yuan and instructed him to tell the abbot Si Bao of the Xin Temple in Dongqiao Village outside the West Gate to borrow 1,600 yuan, which was limited to be paid at Sutai Mountain outside the South Gate on the tenth day of the fifth lunar month.

Hangzhou

Water Pump Delivered to Hangzhou: The Hangzhou Waterworks has signed a contract with the Shanghai Xie Feng Construction Factory for the project and is now scheduled to start construction on the 29th. The two water pumps ordered from Shenchang Foreign Firm at a total price of more than 3,700 yuan were shipped to Hangzhou yesterday.

Qingyun Street Robbery Case Solved: The case of robbery and murder of the woman Yang Fang in the Hengda cigarette shop at the intersection of Qingyun Street, Guanchao, Xiachegn, Hangzhou, has now been solved. It is heard that the provincial capital's detective team has now captured many of the robbers involved in the case and is still investigating and interrogating them.

Ningbo

Butcher Shops Strike to Oppose Slaughterhouse: Yesterday, the butcher shops in Ningbo City went on an informal strike to oppose the Second Slaughterhouse. It is heard that the municipal government believes that the representatives of the butcher shops all supported the construction of the slaughterhouse and did not oppose it. Now that it has been completed, it is difficult to strike against it, and their attitude is very firm.

Yingrui Warship Sails to Dinghai to Be Stationed: The Yingrui warship sailed to Dinghai on May 31 to be stationed to protect the fishing season and patrol for pirates.

Xiaoshan

Preservation of Land Reporting Handling Fees: The Xiaoshan County Government yesterday received an order from Director Zhu of the Civil Affairs Department, stating that although the county's Land Reporting Office had been ordered to close and dissolve completely by the end of April, the second step of the reporting process still needs to continue. All handling fees collected by the county for land reporting, in addition to the four-tenths that should be submitted to the province as previously ordered, the remaining three-tenths retained by the county must be properly preserved for future use and not diverted for other purposes.

Shangnan Township Expedites Disaster Relief: The townships of Shangnan, Xiaoshan, Heshan, Datong, Zixia, etc., suffered repeated disasters last year, with no grain harvested from the fields. Now, during the lean season, the disaster victims are emaciated and pitiful. Local gentry and people have raised 2,000 yuan in cash to purchase 200 dan of cheap rice for distribution, scheduled to begin on June 10th.

Arrangement of Xianghu Yahu Mountain: Since Xianghu Lake in Xiaoshan was developed as a rural normal school and agricultural experiment station, it has achieved considerable success. Now, the graves in the Yahu Mountain area are being ordered to be moved to facilitate the construction of new buildings for farm expansion. The scenery of the lake is excellent, and the future arrangement of buildings and construction to enhance the scenery will be no less appealing to visitors than Hangzhou's West Lake.
