Sports

Detailed Report of the 9th Far Eastern Games (6)

### China vs. Japan Men's Volleyball Preliminary Round (Xu Minhui) – China Wins 2-1

Unfair Refereeing

(Hui Jing Tong Xun) The preliminary round of the China-Japan volleyball match began at 3:00 PM on the 26th, with referees Mr. Hara and Mr. Sakamoto.

The Chinese volleyball team's style is very different, so few Japanese spectators attended the match. They were confident of victory without a doubt, but the result was unexpected. Our team's players were also confident of victory, so they were not very attentive. Before long, the Japanese team repeatedly pressed and scored points. The score quickly showed Japan with nine points, while China only had three. This was due to their underestimation of the opponent. At this point, they realized they could not be too careless, so they quickly caught up. However, within two or three rounds, the Japanese team had already scored eleven points, and our team had four. After switching sides, our team held an emergency meeting to discuss strategies for facing the opponent. As soon as they restarted, they regained control of the ball. Li Fushen served, and they quickly scored several points, tying the score at eleven. Then, Zeng Jingquan served and scored three consecutive points, putting them ahead of the Japanese team at fourteen to eleven. However, they stopped advancing. The Japanese team repeatedly used flanking tactics, taking advantage of the gaps in our three lines, scoring five consecutive points and catching up to sixteen to fourteen. Our team then called a time-out to break the momentum of the opponent. As expected, when the game restarted, Zhu Zucheng scored three consecutive points, resulting in a score of seventeen to sixteen in our team's favor. Just then, the Japanese team scored a point while serving at the net, catching up with our team again. Xu Heng then caught up with two points, resulting in a score of nineteen to eighteen. At this point, both teams defended their positions tightly, unable to advance. After several exchanges, the Japanese team scored two consecutive points through our three lines. The Chinese supporting team was extremely anxious, as the Japanese referee was biased and openly stole points, repeatedly claiming that our team's hands crossed the net or touched the net. Our team captain protested several times, but to no avail. The spectators were outraged, urging our team not to continue the match. Only after repeated persuasion from our team leaders did they agree to resume the game. The two teams did not make much progress. There were still one or two violations and penalties. The cheering squad continued to scold vehemently. The game ended with Japan winning by a score of twenty-two to twenty.

The Chinese cheering squad was extremely angry. Some wanted to withdraw, while others wanted to stay and see how it would end. Everyone believed that under such unfair officiating, even the best skills would be useless.

The second game began with Chen Xibing scoring three consecutive points, and Cao Tingzan also scoring one point, taking the lead. The Japanese team was flustered and reinvigorated, attacking with two lines on the right flank several times. Our team's five generals, Zhu, Li, Xu, Li, and Zeng, were all defeated and returned with no points. Fortunately, our team's Qiu Guangxie and Li Lianying also repelled five enemy generals, so the score remained four to one. The Japanese team scored two more points, and after more than ten battles, there was no clear winner. More than ten minutes passed, but the score was only nine to five. In this game, China often took the lead, and the referee's attitude also changed greatly. Our team members were very calm and able to use their strengths to the fullest. The teamwork was also impressive. When Chen Congchao served, the whole team was invigorated. Qiu Guangxie repeatedly smashed the ball several times. Zhu Zucheng and Li Lianying cooperated to lift the ball in front of the net, slightly higher than the net, and then smashed it down like lightning, scoring eight consecutive points. Although the Japanese team also fought back and regained three points, Cao Tingzan scored four consecutive points while serving. The Japanese team was unable to recover at this point, and China finally won with a score of twenty-one to eight.

In the third game, the Japanese team replaced the right wing player, who was good at smashing, for some reason. In the beginning, the Japanese team still mustered their remaining strength, and the two teams were evenly matched. After a long time, they gradually became tired and exhausted, and the army had no fighting spirit. Our team attacked relentlessly. All those who served returned with points. Among them, Cao Tingzan scored the most points. At twenty to six, Zhu and Li were eager to win and end the game quickly, repeatedly trying to use their superb skills, but they were too hasty and lifted the ball too low, failing repeatedly. Fortunately, the score difference was so large that the Japanese team had no hope of counterattacking. China finally won with a score of twenty-one to eight. Although the Japanese team's ball skills were skillful and young, they were not weak. Their saving ability was very fast, and the smashing balls from the two lines on both wings were also very powerful. Unfortunately, their experience was still small and their training was insufficient, so they ultimately failed.

Our team's Qiu Guangxie made great contributions in this battle. The balls he smashed were either far or near. Although the Japanese team wanted to close the door, he took advantage of the gap to enter, or flew over the enemy's fingers. Most of the points were scored by this gentleman. Zhu and Li's cooperative fast smashing was very distinctive, and the enemy had to admire it.

### China vs. Philippines Football Preliminary Round

China Wins 5-0

Dai Linjing Scores a Hat-Trick and Makes Great Contributions

Zhou Xianyan Bravely Saves the Ball and Achieves Miraculous Results

(Tokyo Communication) On the 27th, at 12:20 PM, the Chinese and Philippine football teams faced off for the first time at the track and field stadium. A crowd of over 50,000 spectators, impressed by the reputation of the two teams, came to watch. The referee was Takechi Torao, with Hamada Satoshi and Asao Yao as linesmen. As a result, China won 3-0 in the first half and 2-0 in the second half. Overall, China won 5-0 against the Philippines. The detailed report of the match is as follows:

(1) Opening the Score in Eight Minutes

After the kickoff, both sides fought bravely. Our side was facing headwinds, so the ball often circled in front of our goal, creating a very dangerous situation. Fortunately, the iron gate Zhou Xianyan guarded it like an iron barrel, otherwise it would have been dangerous. In the eighth minute, our team's right inside forward, Chen Jiaqiu, dribbled the ball straight in, breaking through the inner defensive line to the front of the goal. The Philippine army rushed to pounce, Chen then kicked the ball diagonally, lightly passing it to the center forward Dai Linjing. Dai calmly raised his foot and kicked, quickly and forcefully, directly into the goal from the right corner. The Philippine goalkeeper was unable to defend it. China won the first goal.

(2) Another One in Half an Hour

After that, the Philippine army tried hard to counterattack, and the momentum was quite strong. It had repeatedly taken corner kicks, but to no avail. The Philippine army's forwards' individual skills were not weak, but their teamwork was too lacking. Every time they had a chance to attack the goal, they kicked the ball out of bounds. One time, our team mobilized all its forces, and the interior was empty. Suddenly, the Philippine army's left wing dribbled the ball straight in. Goalkeeper Zhou Xianyan hurriedly left the goal to rescue. The Philippine army's feet were fast, and it was already ten yards away from the goal. Zhou returned and rushed again, but he could not reach it. He only saw the Philippine army raise its foot and kick the ball, but the ball passed over the crossbar, which can be said to be a missed opportunity. At the thirty-first minute, the Philippines was penalized for a corner kick. Ye Beihua kicked it out and the ball landed right in front of the Philippine goal. The soldiers of both sides were mixed in a pile, and the center forward Dai Linjing headed the ball towards the goal, and it went into the net again. Our team won the second goal.

(3) Dai Linjing Scores a Hat-Trick

Only one minute later, Sun Jinshun got the ball and passed it to Ye Beihua, who drove straight towards the goal with the ball, and then passed it to Dai Linjing, whose foot head slightly raised and the ball jumped into the net again. Our team won the third goal. So the cheerleaders sang the song of victory. For days, our country has endured humiliation, and at this time, it was able to vent a little.

(4) The Fourth One Doesn't Count

Since the Philippine army lost two goals, it was still not willing to give up. The whole army launched a general attack to try to attack, but because our team's internal strength was very abundant, there was nothing to do. At the thirty-eighth minute, our army's left wing Ye Beihua got the ball and broke through the enemy's second line of defense. A kick in the wind went into the net again, but the referee came over and said that it was offside and did not count. So the first half ended with our team winning by three to zero.

(5) Ye Beihua Begins to Contribute

After lemon time, the two sides exchanged ground and fought again. Our team replaced Chen Jiaqiu with Chen Guangyao as the right wing, and the power was even more powerful, but the Philippines was not weak and often rushed into the internal defense line. After a long battle, there was no winner. In the twenty-eighth minute, Ye Beihua single-handedly penetrated the enemy territory. From the left, Ye Beihua single-handedly penetrated the enemy territory. From the left, he scored a goal, making the first contribution. Our team won the fourth goal.

(6) Sun Jinshun Gets a Goal

Our army took advantage of the victory to pursue and went all the way, unstoppable. Before a minute had passed, Ye Beihua got the ball and passed it to Sun Jinshun. Sun kicked the ball three times to get close to the goal and kicked the ball into the net from the side corner. Our country won the fifth goal. At this time, our team replaced Ye Beihua with Feng Youyun. The two sides fought fiercely for a long time without any records. As a result, our team won a complete victory with five to zero.

(7) Li Ning's Iron Head Reigns Supreme

In today's battle, every one of our country's team members was as lively as a dragon and a tiger. The Japanese spectators were amazed. In the defense, Li Ning's few lying balls and headers saved many dangerous balls, so the Japanese people honored him as Iron Head. Here is a record of the lineups of the two teams:

China vs. Philippines Second Men's Volleyball Match

China Wins Big 2-0

Avenge the Shame of the First Round Defeat

The second volleyball match between China and the Philippines was held because it was cloudy and rainy, so after the women's exhibition match, the two teams went to the stadium to stretch their muscles and practice slightly. The match was held at 2:45 PM. The referees were Sakamoto and Hirota.

In the first game, the Philippine team served. After two or three smashes, they took a 4-0 lead. Then, the two teams fought each other. Qiu Guangxie's smash was effective. Xu Heng's skillful attack disrupted the enemy's rear. The front row net was also good, and they took a 9-7 lead. However, the tall men in the front row of the Philippine team often lightly jumped and raised their hands to high-pressure balls, which fell vertically and were difficult to save. After switching sides at 11-10, the two teams stole the ball and attacked each other. Their strength was almost equal, and the scores were close. At twenty points, they were tied. Qiu Guangxie's smash was effective, and Li Lianying's spike was effective. As a result, they won with a score of twenty-two to twenty.

In the second game, our team became more and more proud and disturbed the enemy's formation, throwing empty gaps and scoring points with every move. The Philippine army's teamwork was poor, but they also tried hard to cope. After more than ten fierce battles, Qiu Guangxie's quick strike changed the venue at eleven to six. After that, the Philippine team rallied and hit the ball more accurately. Our army's rear guard also lost a lot of ground and chased closely to fifteen to fourteen, almost tying the score. However, the opponent's front row touched the net, and Li Lianying's spike was amazing, increasing the score to eighteen to fourteen. The Philippine team requested time, intending to dampen our sharp edge. In the continued competition, the Philippine team's front row violated the net again. Cao Tingzan and Chen Xibing's smashes gradually made the Philippine team unable to support themselves, and the score was twenty to fifteen. In the last point, both sides desperately attacked and defended. Good skills continued to come out, and there was no compromise back and forth. The battle was extremely fierce, and our team won with a score of twenty-one to fifteen, washing away the shame of the first round defeat and tying the Philippines with one win and one loss.

### China vs. Japan Baseball Preliminary Round

China Suffers a Crushing Defeat 3-21

(Tokyo Communication) The preliminary baseball match between China and Japan was held at 2:30 PM on the 26th. Before the war, our army was highly anticipated. Japanese critics and experts did not dare to underestimate the strength of the Honolulu Chinese team, so baseball fans rushed to the stadium to watch. Unexpectedly, the two teams' ball skills were far apart. The Japanese army wreaked havoc, and China was at a loss. The Japanese audience was delighted, but our army's supporters were heartbroken and extremely sad.

In the competition, I only saw the Japanese army active and rampant, attacking fiercely. In the first inning, our team's pitcher, Zhong You, controlled the ball quite well and killed two enemies first. However, due to careless defense, Japan scored two people on base. When the score was two to three, the enemy's strong third base right-side ball rolled far to the left wing and became a home run, scoring three points in one fell swoop. The decline of our team's morale probably started from this. After that, in each inning, Japan became more violent and attacked with all its forces, while our team's defense gradually collapsed and mistakes were made one after another. By the time the enemy scored thirteen points, in the fourth inning, our team recovered two points. In the fifth, sixth, and seventh innings, the Japanese added eight points, and the overall situation was decided. In the sixth inning, Chen Yunfang was transferred to pitcher, but it was difficult to stop the enemy's power. In the eighth inning, Cai Yunping, who took over, could not bear it and took the heavy responsibility of pitcher. Yu Xian was the catcher, and he was able to do nothing. As a result, Japan won a great victory with twenty-one points to three. Alas, China's defeat.

Japan vs. Philippines Second Men's Volleyball Match

Philippines Wins Big 2-0

(Tokyo Communication) The second volleyball match between the Philippines and Japan was held on the 27th at 3:55 PM in the rain. The referee was Toyoshima Sakamoto, and the Japanese army served first.

In the first game, Japan lost the right to serve due to touching the net. The Philippine team's front-row pressure attack and slashing tactics scored points with every move. The Japanese army was not weak and chased closely behind. The Philippines switched sides at eleven to eight. Japan switched Wu and Sakagami to join the army, and the military might was quite strong. In an instant, they tied the score at fourteen points. After that, they took a 17-16 lead. However, this effort was only momentary. The Philippine team's slash became sharper and the net was sure. In the end, they won with a score of 21-17.

In the second game, Japan was quite superior at first. The two armies were very busy pressing and attacking, and they dealt with each other for a long time. Moreover, the rain made the game difficult due to the wet ball. After a tie of nine points, the front row center of the Philippine team used their tall stature and long arms to slash and score, switching sides at eleven to nine. After entering, the battle was fierce. It was not easy to score points back and forth. However, the Japanese army made continuous mistakes because they were eager to recover. The Philippine team took advantage of the situation to attack sharply and won a victory with a score of 21 to 12.

### China vs. Philippines Second Baseball Match

China Wins Big 15-4

(Tokyo Communication) The second baseball match between China and the Philippines was held on the 28th at 2:30 PM. Black clouds covered the stadium. Because it had rained the previous day, it was wet, and the strength of the three baseball countries had already been determined in the preliminary match between China and Japan, so there were very few spectators.

Our team attacked first. In the first inning, Zhang Rong'an saw the ball go out of bounds. The next player had a hit and four balls filled the bases. Cheng Guanbing hit a long shot to the right wing and scored the first point. The Philippine team had three unproductive players. In the second inning, neither side scored. In the third inning, Lu Shujie hit the ball and got on base. With the help of his teammates, he scored another point. In the fourth inning, Zhang Rong'an hit a double to send Feng Enci back to the team for one point. The Philippine team changed pitchers. Feng Yuhe hit the enemy's right wing. The front ball was lost and rolled far to become a triple. Zhang Rong'an scored. The Philippine team also took advantage of our team's mistakes to retaliate with two points. In the sixth inning, when our team was full of bases, the enemy advanced to defend. Feng Yuhe broke through the shortstop and both ran back to the team. Cai Yunping hit a left-field single and sent his teammates back to report a point. At this time, he changed pitchers again. Cheng Guanbing made a high fly sacrifice hit, and Feng Yuhe ran back quickly. He Donghan intercepted Cai Yunping's score in front of the first base line. In this turbulent game, our team scored five points in one fell swoop. In the seventh inning, they continued to attack fiercely and added two points. The overall situation had been decided. The Philippine team worked hard to win two points with two hits. In the ninth inning, in the final battle, the Chinese athletes wreaked havoc and scored more points. In conclusion, they won a great victory with a score of fifteen to four.

Anecdotes from the Games

New Record for Athlete Age

On the first day of the Games, many new records were set, and the most interesting was the new record for athlete age. Some say that Mr. Feng Enci, a Chinese baseball player, is 54 years old, while others say he is 47 years old. He is roughly around 50 years old and has grandchildren. Unexpectedly, things are never so unique. Mrs. Asabuki, a Japanese tennis player, is definitely not young either. She is 42 years old this year, and her son has already entered Keio University. These two are old oddities. There is also one who is surprisingly young, namely the Philippine baseball player S, who is only eleven years old this year. The big bat is bigger than

Bottom corner from left to right: Li Xinghua, Li Mudan, Enge Yue, Garrico

he is, and he actually enters and exits international sports venues. These two are records that have never been seen since the beginning of the Far Eastern Games.

Girls Yelling "Mr. Kimura"

The Philippine high jumper, Toku, jumped to two meters in one breath, which stunned most people and left them speechless. The Japanese athlete Kimura was also not bad, jumping over one meter and ninety-six centimeters, but at this time, he was a little hesitant and unsure whether to jump again or stop here. He couldn't make up his mind. Later, he failed once and didn't pass twice. In the end, he couldn't get excited for the third time. At that time, the whole field was silent, watching what would happen. Unexpectedly, a group of female students next to him yelled "Mr. Kimura," breaking the air.

Cheerleading Squad Shines Alone

In the various competition venues of the outer garden, it can be said that you can't see the small flags of green, white, and red all over the ground here. Among the spectators, there is a pile of red hats in the east and a pile of white hats in the west, all of which are our country's cheerleading squad. There are countless other plainclothes teams. From the moment the athletes enter the venue, they start working, shouting slogans and singing cheering songs. This side says "China," and the other side continues with "Hua," followed by shouting "Long live" in unison. This rises and the other falls, without a moment of rest, making the atmosphere in the whole field tense to the extreme and excited to the extreme. It's really rare to be so energetic.

Don't Be Sordid, but Be Hilarious

Before the first China-Japan basketball game started, the athletes from both countries went to the stadium to practice. The Chinese athletes wore white clothes, white pants, and white shoes, plus the red national emblem on their chests, which was extremely bright. The Japanese athletes were all in gray clothes and pants. A Japanese girl next to them said, "They look as sordid as mice." After a while, both sides took off their coats. The Japanese athletes also looked very beautiful in yellow clothes and white pants. A Chinese person said to the little girl, "Don't be sordid." This made everyone laugh heartily, and the little girl couldn't help but smile.

Solving the Problem of Young People's Further Education: A Guide to Further Education is About to be Published

During the summer vacation, choosing a school is the most important issue for young people pursuing further education. If there is no reference material, our institute has spent two months investigating 103 of the most famous schools in various parts of the country (35 universities, 17 vocational schools, 36 secondary schools, 10 vocational schools, and 5 normal schools). Our institute adheres to the principle of preferring quality over quantity and has compiled the latest content, composition, departments, teachers, graduation deadlines, application qualifications and procedures, detailed tuition fees per semester, and the current recruitment methods of each school. All information is based on facts and is not concealed. At the end, the admission advertisements of each school are attached for easy comparison and search. Young people pursuing further education should have a copy on hand. The exquisite hardcover book costs 15 cents to cover the printing costs. Please send letters for postal purchase. The book will be sent as soon as it is published. Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center, 442 Lafayette Road, Qi, Wu Te 1456

The United States is Actively Preparing for the 10th

World Games

The 10th World Games will be held in Los Angeles, USA, in 1932. The flags of the conference, which promote peace and friendship, will soon be hung high in the stadiums of Los Angeles, fluttering in the wind to show the integration of people from all over the world who love each other.

The Initiator Sows Seeds and Harvests

In 1894, Baron Pierre de Coubertin of France, based on his innate love for peace and friendship, initiated this great World Games. It has gradually developed, and 62 countries have registered as members. This brilliant phenomenon in modern sports history is the first step in the initiator's sowing of seeds and harvesting.

The United States is Actively Preparing

Since Los Angeles was designated as the venue for the next Games at the closing of the previous session, the residents of the city and people across the United States have considered it an honor of the era. They have concentrated the talents of national sports institutions, organized various committees, and worked hard to prepare. The three famous American presidents Harding, Coolidge, and Hoover have been deeply interested and have expressed their warm sympathy in letters. The president of Harvard University said that this kind of integration of friendship circulating in the Games can directly foster human sympathy and understanding.

China Must Prepare Quickly

China is also one of the 62 member countries of the Games. The representative of the Games is Dr. Wang Zhengting. At the previous session (9th session), our country sent representative Song Ruhai to participate in the grand ceremony. The 10th session will be held in two years. It is hoped that the sports community in our country will make a determination, work hard to prepare quickly, so that there will also be Chinese athletes competing in the next Games.

Zhang Zhijiang Will Return to China from Japan

Arriving in Shanghai on the 7th of this month

Part of the Librarians Stay in Japan for Inspection

Zhang Zhijiang, curator of the Central Guoshu Institute, in order to have a reference for the boxing category in this Far Eastern Games held in Japan, led a group of ten members of the institute, including Zhu Guofu, to travel to Japan to attend the meeting, as has been previously reported. Now it is known that Zhang, the meeting having concluded, except for some members of the institute who will stay in Japan to inspect the country's jujutsu swordsmanship, it is heard that Zhang himself and three others, including Zhu Guofu, have already left to return to China. It is estimated that the journey will take approximately to arrive in Shanghai around the 7th of this month.

Important News

Ministry of Education Order

Abolition of University Preparatory Courses

The Ministry of Education reiterates the order to abolish university preparatory courses, instructing educational departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities, as well as universities. It states that establishing preparatory courses in universities easily leads to abuses. A notice was previously issued to all universities, stating that they must not enroll preparatory students from the 19th year of the Republic onward. Now that the summer vacation is approaching, the previous order is reiterated. If any school deliberately violates the order, the local educational administrative authorities should strictly prohibit any established private universities from doing so. Regarding unestablished private universities, the Ministry will not accept applications for establishment from those that enrolled preparatory students in the 19th year. In addition to separate orders, this order is issued for compliance.

Su (Jiangsu) Education Department

Second Day of Meeting to Transfer and Investigate Education Bureau Chiefs

The second meeting of the Jiangsu Education Department to transfer and investigate education bureau chiefs of various counties was held yesterday. The previous day's proceedings were reported yesterday. Today, general meetings were held in the morning and afternoon. Before the morning meeting, section chiefs Duan Fuqun and Yang Xin from the Education Department gave speeches. It was originally planned to invite Ye Xiufeng, member of the Provincial Party Affairs Reorganization Committee, to give a speech in the afternoon, but due to Ye's other important engagements, the speech was postponed.

The minutes of the second meeting are as follows: Chairman: Director Chen (Yang Naikang, substitute), Recorder: Yang Changyun, Huang Rujian. After the formal greetings, the chairman delivered a speech, followed by a speech from Section Chief Duan, and a report on relevant matters. 1. The Party Ideology Education Group reported on the review process. 2. The Secondary Education Group reported on the review process. Matters for discussion: Party Ideology Education Group. 1. Proposal on remedial measures for the insufficient number of Party Ideology teachers. It was resolved that, with reference to the resolution of the previous session of bureau chiefs' meeting, the Education Department should cooperate with the Provincial Party Headquarters to organize a Party Ideology Teacher Verification Committee, and request that it hold a verification test for Party Ideology teachers and directors of moral education in primary and secondary schools in the shortest possible time. The Education Department or the Party Ideology Teacher Verification Committee should notify the education bureaus of each county and inform all schools, encouraging party members among the teachers to register for the verification test as much as possible.

1. Proposal on the allocation and addition of Party Ideology courses. It was resolved that before the central government promulgates the standards for Party Ideology courses, the allocation and implementation should be temporarily governed by the interim general rules for Party Ideology courses and Instruction No. 486 of the Education Department. 1. Proposal on the study of teaching methods for Party Ideology courses. It was resolved that the teaching methods for Party Ideology courses should be handled with reference to the resolution of the first session of bureau chiefs' meeting on this matter, with emphasis on the arrangement of the Party Ideology environment. 1. Proposal on the selection of implementation methods for moral education in elementary schools. It was resolved that before the central government promulgates the standards for moral education, the education bureau of each county should formulate a plan for the implementation of moral education in accordance with the educational purpose and submit it to the Education Department for review. Secondary Education Group. 1. Proposal on how to investigate, statistically analyze, guide, and promote higher specialized talents in each county. It was resolved that this case had been discussed and resolved in the first session of the bureau chiefs' meeting, so there was no need to discuss it again. 1. Proposal on how to effectively rectify and reorganize normal education in each county. It was resolved that A. County-level normal schools should pay special attention to rural education and increase agricultural equipment or cooperate with local agricultural institutions to facilitate agricultural practice. B. Please stipulate the service years of normal school graduates and promulgate the service regulations for implementation. C. D. Promulgate and implement the plan. 1. Proposal on how to reorganize and improve junior high schools in each county. Matters for discussion: Education Administration Group. 1. Proposal by the Education Department to the Ministry of Education to revise the methods for the appointment of principals of county-level primary and secondary schools and directors of social education institutions. It was resolved that (1) The appointment of principals of municipal and county-level secondary schools and directors of social education institutions should be based on the recommendation of qualified personnel by the municipal and county education bureaus, who should then be reported to the municipal and county governments and forwarded to the provincial education department for approval and appointment. (2) The principals of municipal and county-level primary schools should be selected and appointed by the municipal and county education bureau chiefs, and separately reported to the municipal and county governments and the provincial education department for review.

Regulations on Researching Party Ideology and Assessing Teaching Staff

The Ministry of Education, in accordance with the Central Executive Committee's Training Department letter, issued the Regulations on Researching Party Ideology and Assessing Teaching Staff in Schools at All Levels, along with the Reporting Form Template, to the educational departments and bureaus of all provinces and cities, stating:

Approved, the Central Report Committee Training Department's letter No. 889 states: "The Provisional Regulations on the Research of Party Ideology by Teaching Staff in Schools at All Levels, previously formulated by this department, have been sent to your ministry for promulgation and compliance. Now, in order to promote research, this department has formulated the Regulations on Researching Party Ideology and Assessing Teaching Staff in Schools at All Levels, and two types of Reporting Form Templates for Researching Party Ideology by Teaching Staff in Schools at All Levels for assessment purposes. In addition to ordering the training departments of the party headquarters in all provinces and cities to comply, we have attached the aforementioned regulations and reporting form templates to this letter for your review and forwarding to educational administrative organs and schools at all levels for compliance and feedback." Attached are two copies each of the Regulations on Researching Party Ideology and Assessing Teaching Staff in Schools at All Levels and the Reporting Form Template for Researching Party Ideology and Assessing Teaching Staff in Schools at All Levels. Approved by the Ministry, in addition to separate orders, the original regulations and reporting form templates are printed and issued for compliance and forwarding to all subordinates for compliance.

Regulations on Researching Party Ideology and Assessing Teaching Staff in Schools at All Levels Article 1 These regulations are formulated in accordance with Article 6 of the Provisional Regulations on Researching Party Ideology by Teaching Staff in Schools at All Levels. Article 2 The performance of research on Party Ideology by teaching staff in schools at all levels shall be assessed by the competent authority and the training department of the party headquarters at the same level. However, for practical convenience, the training department of the party headquarters may designate its subordinate training department to conduct the assessment. Article 3 The assessment of the performance of research on Party Ideology by teaching staff in schools at all levels shall be conducted in the following two ways: 1. Formulate a "Reporting Form for the Performance of Research on Party Ideology by Teaching Staff in Schools at All Levels," distribute it to the principals of each school, and fill it out and submit it on a regular basis. 2. Send personnel to conduct actual assessments or hold tests. Article 4 At the beginning of each semester, the training department of the party headquarters at all levels shall notify each school of the assessment of the performance of research on Party Ideology by the teaching staff in each school in the previous semester, and send it to the competent authority for reference. Article 5 The training department of the party headquarters at all levels shall report the results of the assessment to the training department of the party headquarters at the higher level on a regular basis. Article 6 The training department of the party headquarters at all levels shall report the teaching staff with excellent performance to the training department of the party headquarters at the higher level for appropriate awards. Article 7 Matters not covered by these regulations shall be revised by the Central Training Department. Article 8 These regulations shall be promulgated and implemented by the Central Report Committee Training Department.

Su (Jiangsu) Education Department

Order Prohibiting Education Bureau Chiefs from Leaving Office Lightly

Jiangsu Provincial Education Department Instruction No. 824, Order to the education bureau chiefs of each county, states: For the purpose of compliance, it has been observed that the education bureau chiefs of various counties often resign due to minor difficulties or other obstacles, and some even entrust the bureau affairs to a substitute and leave their posts without prior approval. This has a significant impact on local education and is a failure to take public service seriously. From now on, the education bureau chiefs of each county must wait until the newly appointed bureau chief takes over before they are allowed to leave the county. Absolutely no one is allowed to leave their post without handing over the affairs and being irresponsible before the handover. Anyone who dares to violate this will be severely investigated. In addition to separate orders, this order is urgently issued for compliance, without fail.

During the Municipal Education Bureau's Office Meeting

Director Chen's Important Report

Director Chen of the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau reported at the 155th Office Meeting: (1) This month, due to the need to hold the entrance examination and other business, the work is relatively stressful. However, the purpose of the bureau in holding the entrance examination is simply to reorganize the education in this city and has no other purpose. However, the outside world does not understand the truth and has generated many rumors that the entrance examination is a prelude to suppression and takeover. However, I believe that to do things, one must have a firm determination, and rumors can be ignored. Therefore, no matter how difficult the entrance examination is, it must be carried out according to the established plan. If any school does not comply with the order, it will be punished accordingly. Even if this causes a great storm, I will accept it. There are many veteran educators in this city who, whenever an accident occurs, take the opportunity to make trouble and obstruct progress. Therefore, the inability to manage education in this city is actually affected by these educators. I have the responsibility and determination to reorganize education and will not shrink back in order to promote the development of education. I hope everyone will pay attention to this determination. (2) There are not many days left in this year, but there are still many tasks that have not been completed. The work seems to be too slow. It must be known that if anyone does not work hard, it will affect everyone from the director of the bureau to the clerk. If such a chronic disease is found in any staff member in the future, I will only enforce the law and will not be lenient. I hope the section chiefs will warn their colleagues to pay close attention. (3) From now on, staff attendance must be handled in accordance with the attendance rules. Senior personnel must also report to the director's office, and junior personnel must fill out attendance forms for assessment. Otherwise, the actions are too free and the discipline is too lax. Therefore, I solemnly declare that attention must be paid. (4) The end of this year is approaching. Various businesses within the scope of this year must also come to an end. I hope the sections and departments will carefully consider and complete them as soon as possible so that they can be clearly separated from the work of the next year. If there are not enough personnel, it is better to hire temporary personnel to help. Therefore, the office hours this month will be extended by one hour each day. It must be known that the situation in China is different from that in Europe and the United States. Under the current state of affairs in China, we can only use a sincere attitude and full energy to strive for the vigorous advancement of our cause, and we cannot imitate Europe and the United States in evenly distributing office hours, rest, and entertainment time.

Ma Guli Gives a Lecture at the China Academy of Arts

Dr. Ma Guli has always attached great importance to the literature and art of our country. The other day, he visited the China Academy of Arts (formerly known as the China Academy of Literature and Art) at the Ningbo Fellow Association and deeply appreciated the exhibition of works by teachers and students. Yesterday, he gave a lecture at the school accompanied by Dr. Ding Zhaoqing and Liu Suijiu, the founders of the school. Professors Zhang Hongwei, Ma Mengrong, Ma Gongyu, Zheng Manqing, and Fang Jiean entertained him. The main idea of the speech was that Chinese painting has always focused on freehand brushwork, while Western painting has always focused on realism, with the ability to resemble the real as the goal. However, after the invention of photography, it was realized that realism is not the ultimate goal of art, and the value of freehand brushwork was gradually understood. Therefore, European art today is gradually becoming Chinese. The words were very pertinent. After the speech, Liu Suijiu and Ding Zhaoqing gave speeches to further elaborate on Dr. Ma's ideas.

College Guidance to be Published

During the summer vacation, the most important issue for college-bound youths is to choose a school, but there is a lack of reference materials. The Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center spent two months investigating 103 of the most famous schools in various parts of the country (35 universities, 17 vocational schools, 36 middle schools, 10 vocational schools, and 5 normal schools). Based on the principle of rather have less than poor quality, the latest content, organization, departmental teachers, graduation deadlines, and admission qualifications and procedures, the cost per semester, and the detailed recruitment methods for this year are listed in detail, all of which are factual and not concealed. At the end, the recruitment advertisements of each school this year are attached, which is easy to compare and convenient to check. The book is suitable for college-bound youths to have one copy in hand. The hard-bound book costs 15 cents to recover the printing fee. Letters and postal orders will be mailed immediately after publication.

Eulogy to the Martyrs of Lakeside Chen Boying

Eulogy to the Martyrs of Lakeside is written to mourn the martyr Chen Ying shi. His courtesy name was Qimei, a native of Wuxing. He learned business as a child and went to Japan to study at the age of thirty. In the winter of that year, he joined the Tongmenghui. In the autumn of Xinhai, the Wuchang Uprising broke out. Jun led his comrades to attack the Shanghai Manufacturing Bureau and broke it. The public then elected him as the Governor of the Shanghai Army. In the first year of the Republic of China, Yuan Shikai appointed him as the Minister of Industry and Commerce, but he refused and strongly opposed him. Several uprisings were unsuccessful. Yuan was afraid of him and sent his party to assassinate him in his residence, and he was killed. It was May 18th, the fifth year of the Republic of China. His tomb is located on the shore of Bilang Lake, beside the Xian Mountain, two or three miles outside the South Gate of Huzhou. I went to pay my respects more than ten days after this year's commemoration. There is a stone archway in front of the tomb. The front plaque is inscribed with the words "Achieving Benevolence and Taking Righteousness". There are couplets on the sides, saying, "Anecdotes are enough to prove that they can supplement the biographies of roaming heroes and merchants. Former sages are not allowed to let them, and they are indeed the first-class of Lu Lianzi and Fang." The back plaque says, "Gong De Feng Cen". The couplet says, "A grave buries Huang Chang, walking near Xian Mountain and shedding tears together. Three years of hiding Bixue, the sound is sad, Du Yuhe Zhao soul." Entering the lane, small trees are planted, half the height of a person. Entering again is the tomb gate. Passing the tomb gate is the tomb. The two sides are like embracing each other. There is a couplet saying, "Supporting the top and holding the danger, the cause is shining like the sun and the moon. Achieving benevolence and taking righteousness, looking up and down without shame, both heaven and man." There is a monument on it, inscribed with the words "The Tomb of Chen Gong Ying Shi", written by the former Premier. In front of the tomb are the words "The Spirit Is As Strong As Mountains And Rivers". The four walls are engraved with elegies and elegies, which cannot be fully recorded. The tomb is made of stone, simple and solemn, making people awe-inspiring. At that time, the color of the sun was slightly tragic, and a long wind came from the lake. Looking at the four mountains, it was like holding arms and waiting for them. There was no one else who came to the tomb. Thinking of the vastness of heaven and earth, calling the hero but not rising, all kinds of feelings were intertwined, and I couldn't help but linger for a long time. There is a ridge to the east of the tomb, and there is a pavilion on the ridge called Xiongkua Pavilion. There is a couplet saying, "The forests and valleys of the peaks in the southwest are especially beautiful. On the good days of spring and autumn, singing and weeping here." It is a collection of sentences, and it is neat and elegant, which can be called seamless. The first and last words are embedded in its beauty and the four characters of Dangsi are especially ingenious and cannot be achieved. The writer also put a lot of thought into it. After I came down, I regretted not bringing a pot of wine to pay tribute to the secluded spirit. After returning, I picked up a pen and wrote it down.

A Toad Weighing Five Pounds Clear and Thin

A few days ago, my friend Zhang Fulou told me that he had personally seen a native of Loudong get an extremely large toad, that is, he wanted to name the toad a "Lai Tuan," weighing more than five catties. The natives regarded it as a rare commodity and entered the city, hoping to get a good price for it. Some advised him to sell it to the pharmacy, which would definitely get a high price, but he did not succeed. Later, it was seen in a tea house in the city by a kind person who spent money to buy it and released it in the backyard to live in it, and allowed people to watch it. According to Yun, its thing is huge and unmatched, and it is like a turtle at first glance. Its hind feet are red and shiny, and the piles on its back are high and super like graves. They are all amazed as never seen before. Yu heard that foreign black people who travel far in the desert always cover their faces with Lai Tuan skin, feeling cool and incomparable. This thing is afraid of sunlight, and its body secretes a kind of viscous liquid from time to time to avoid it, so there is this utilization. Also, according to the Nanshi Yin Yan Biography, when the Western Expedition was made, large toad carts were made to carry scholars and cowhide to cover them, and pushed them to fill the trenches. It is clear that this thing has been created by those who have been in charge of the steering wheel, and it is not the creation of today.

Flower Planting Fair Notes Sheng Huang Yingdai

In recent years, there have been flower planting fairs held in Shanghai. Chinese and Western famous flowers are gathered in one room, and flower lovers are all excited to engage in evaluation. On May 29th, there was another spring flower planting fair, and the location was at the Dahua Hotel. The situation in the field is briefly described below.

On this day, Chinese and Western famous flowers were gathered in the field. Among them, five pansies were planted in small sky-blue flower pots, half purple and half yellow, short and small, and beautiful to watch. Among them, the tower of dianthus was decorated in a unique way, with tropical flowers and various palm leaves at the four corners. Various spring flower planting, colorful, bright and dazzling. The Italian Garden has been closed since the autumn flower planting fair, and this time various famous flowers have been added to the exhibition, among which the roses are the best. Others, such as pale purple caper flowers and golden longevity chrysanthemums, are set off by the emerald green grass, which makes them feel more fresh and makes people happy. A bunch of Rafant grass is placed in the center of the ball center. White butterfly flowers are slender and drooping, and the tables and chairs placed in the room are also moved out on this day to facilitate the display of flower planting. Other creeping grasses, daisies, etc. are arranged in neat rows and arranged properly. As for the tables in the garden, they are full of potted flowers, all of which are famous species. The most eye-catching is a table covered with embroidered tablecloths, with a flower basket placed on it, which is said to be the product of a certain school. Among the flowers placed in the basket, the golden yellow roses are the most precious. On the afternoon of this day, the guests gathered together. The costumes of Chinese women were unique, with long and short cheongsams of different colors, and the shadows of hairpins and hairpins were extremely prosperous for a while. And some female students from a certain school came to visit in blue cloth uniforms and small hats. It was also heard that Mr. Tang Shaoyi also came to visit on this day. Finally, Chinese and Western experts made evaluations, and most of the winners were planted by Western women.

Rain Blocks the Huxin Temple National Walking Group Liu Hanru

It has been three months since we set off. We have passed through a total of sixteen counties of all sizes. We arrived in Huaian, Jiangbei on National Humiliation Day. Recalling the daily life of these three months, we have not felt any hardship. And all comrades are physically strong and mentally active, which is worthy of comforting those who care about us. For the past three months, we have been running around and have not had a chance to rest. This time, we arrived in Huaian and, with the introduction of County Magistrate Wang Zhenyu, we were able to stay in the Huxin Temple in Meili for a few days, to sort out our work and take a little rest before moving on. The temple is located three miles west of the city of Huaian, with clear water and wood, and the halls and pavilions are solemn. Although it is not as large as Lingyin, the scenery is really good. At the entrance, there is a horizontal plaque that says "Huxin Suoyue", the anonymous person's surname is very similar to the handwriting of Qing Daoren. On the reverse side of the plaque, it says "Youji Keyuan", which was inscribed by Wu Changshuo. In the middle of the Kangxi period, Emperor Renmiao made a southern tour and personally wrote the three characters "Youji Temple" and gave it to the temple monks, so it is also known as Youji Temple. Outside the temple, there is a two-hundred-meter-long forest on the right side, and the same on the left side. Entering the temple gate, you must pass over a small bridge. On the opposite side of the bridge, there is also a plaque that says "City Mountain Forest", which was written by Zheng Xiaoxu. Outside the temple gate, in addition to the forest, there is also a vast courtyard, covering several acres, all planted with vegetables, called "Guachou", "Yuqu", and "Caiqi". The abbot's room is elegantly furnished, and the walls are full of calligraphy and paintings by celebrities. Abbot Hui specially opened the Mengjiao Mountain Room on the side of the Baojing Hall for us to stay. We ordinary vulgar people occupy the pure Buddhist land, which is very uneasy. On the evening of the 14th, Abbot Hui set up a vegetarian feast to wash us down. During the banquet, he talked about the history of the temple, and only then did we know that the temple was built in the Tang Dynasty and flourished in the early Ming Dynasty.

There were only a few thatched huts, and the address was originally named Guanjia Lake. The temple is located in the heart of the lake, so it is named Huxin Temple. In the Jiawu year of Qianlong, the Lao Ba Kou River burst, and the river was silted up and leveled. After several repairs, it has the scale it is today. At the end, he presented a volume of Huxin inscriptions, all of which were poems left by famous people of the time. Being in this pure land, untouched by vulgar dust, hearing the sound of the Qing, makes the vulgar people have the thought of breaking away from everything and converting to the Three Jewels. We have been living here for a week, and we have been blocked by rain, which has prevented us from moving forward. Once the weather clears, we will go to Qingjiang. We have been greatly favored by the people from all walks of life in Huai'an, who have either given us lavish banquets or given us guidance and support, as well as the hospitality of County Magistrate Wang and the kindness of Abbot Hui, all of which are appreciated.

The Battle of Throwing Stones in Lanxi

Reading Mr. Gu Shide's article "The Stone-Throwing Festival" in a previous issue of this publication, one learns that this custom is not unique to Guangdong. However, whether this practice can truly avert disaster is something the author cannot know, sharing the same doubt as ascending heights on the Double Ninth Festival.

When the author was young, he would accompany elders to climb "Lianfeng Mountain" in Zhongshan. The scenery there was extremely serene and secluded. Looking down from the mountain, the roofs of houses resembled fish scales, and the fields were far away. The battle of throwing stones would invariably take place here every year. When the sun rose high in the sky, tourists gathered like ants. The two warring factions would each prepare large and small sharp stones as weapons, lying in wait at either end of the mountain. They would wait for the main combatant to light firecrackers, while spectators stood on the slopes, watching the outcome. The two sides would frequently hurl stones at each other in a rapid back-and-forth, with loud shouts to display their courage. Timid spectators, though highly interested, were also afraid of stray stones, so they watched with their heads covered. Those who cheered as if celebrating a victory. When one side ran out of stones, they would be in a dangerous situation, as the enemy would relentlessly pursue with stones, like wild horses charging across the mountain, causing broken heads and injured bodies. The results were often shocking. Those who sustained injuries not only did not feel distressed but even felt exhilarated, stopping the bleeding with yellow smoke. Their heroic spirit was enough to inspire the weak.

If one side was willing to admit defeat, they would raise a white flag as a sign of surrender, and the opposing side would wait for the main combatant to light firecrackers before ceasing hostilities.

After the battle, a banquet would typically be held. If there was no animosity between the two sides and it was merely a friendly competition, the victorious team would host a banquet for the defeated team, and they would celebrate together, not treating each other as enemies. If the battle was caused by revenge, the defeated party would offer a banquet as a sign of apology and as a congratulatory gift.

This kind of large-scale warfare was prevalent among the lower classes, but the upper classes did not engage in it, as the benefits were few and the harm was great, with injuries being inevitable. In recent years, Zhongshan County has vigorously reformed old customs, and it is unknown whether this kind of useless practice has been eliminated.

(P.S.) Mr. Gu's "My Village," I wonder which village it is? Please enlighten me.

Theater News from Xindu: Xu Xiaoting

The National Grand Theater of Xindu is located at a suitable location in Huapailou. Its construction is magnificent, and its facilities are complete. It is the only cinema in Xindu. This time, at the request of local residents Mr. Peng and Mr. Zhang, it made an exception to rent the place for a Mandarin opera performance to raise funds. Among those in charge are Mr. Sun Bowen, the commander of the Jiangning Fortress, and other famous figures. They specially invited Mr. Su Shaoqing to serve as the casting director. The dates are set for June 5th, 6th, and 7th, with six day and night performances, creating an unprecedented spectacle in Xindu. The repertoire has been set: Jin Shaoshan and Rui Debao's complete "Chain Trap," Jin Shaoshan and Xu Ziyi's (a famous amateur Tan-style beards from Nanjing) "Famen Temple," Jin Shaoshan and Liu Zhongqiu's (Shaoqing's talented student who collaborated with Bao Xiaodie at the Great China Company to record the "South Heaven Gate" record) "Yu Zangjian Assassinating King Liao," Jin Shaoshan's "Herding Tigers Pass," Rui Debao's "Picking the Flower Cart," "Ancient City Meeting," "Huarong Road," "Single Plank Bridge Pass," Zhang Wanyun and Jia Futang's (a famous amateur from Beiping who is on par with Qiu Guixian and is currently a storyteller for the China Public Theater) "Second Entry to the Palace," Zhuo Youqi's "Chengdu Zhaoguan Cursing Cao Tanning Mother," Guangdong female amateur Zheng Menglan's three Cantonese operas, and Kunqu operas such as Xu Laotaitai's "Wandering in the Garden," "Sweeping the Flowers," "Yearning for the Mortal World," and "Auspicious Date Making a Scene." In addition, there will be Beijing operas by famous amateurs from Su, Chang, Ning, and Xi. Because Shaoqing has to take care of everything, he will only perform in "Empty City Stratagem," with Shaoshan playing Ma Su, Debao accompanying Wang Ping, and Futang playing Sima Yi. This combination of talent is truly rare. The musicians are the two masters Sun Zuochen and Chen Yanheng, and the drummers are Yang Yulou and Luo Zhongquan, which makes it even more wonderful. Xindu has a population of three million people and has long suffered from a lack of theater. This large-scale performance will surely cause a sensation throughout the city. (Gratitude)

Warmth in the Heart (II)(O)(VI) Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Eleven: Green Curtains and Pearl Hairpins, Fair Lady Returns to a Fine Gentleman; Jade Pendants and Crimson Bed Curtains, Famous Courtesan Marries into a Prominent Family

Speaking to that point, Liu Xingshu smiled and said, "This has again sparked a round of your empty theories. I asked which of the three suitors, Ruiyun, is the best. According to what you've said, Ruiyun's heart must naturally be most inclined towards the youngest, Zhao Qi." Zuo Shuchen said, "This is just my personal conjecture. In any case, property is not an issue among the three conditions I mentioned. I've heard that all three are wealthy and are gentlemen of high standing. It's just that I don't know about the third issue I mentioned." Liu Xingshu said, "Why don't you try to find out? Did she marry that one? Are you not concerned at all? I'm very worried about it." Zuo Shichen said, "It's not that I'm not concerned, but I've been busy these past few days, so I haven't seen Ruiyun, and it's not good to ask her too eagerly. I'll naturally know when the festival arrives. But in these few days, I do want to go once to find out." After saying this, two more days passed, and Zuo Shichen went to Ruiyun's place. It was only five or six days away from the festival, but there were fewer and fewer customers in the tea rooms. The Shanghai business community values the three major festivals of the year, and there is a slight lull near the festivals, so they are inevitably a little busy. Secondly, there is a custom in the courtesan houses that hand towels must be paid for near the festivals. Usually, a towel is provided by the room attendants, but near the festivals, the towels are sent from the assistants. After the customers wipe with the towels, there is a customary reward. It's not that the towel is anything special, but it's a kind of hint for festival rewards. At that time, customers will take out reward envelopes of ten or twenty dollars. This towel later had a nickname called "Ciba Dumplings." This is just a towel, named after its shape. Some thrifty customers are afraid of eating Ciba dumplings, so they usually run very diligently, but they don't come during these few days. Therefore, the courtesan houses are much more idle. Zuo Shichen arrived at Ruiyun's place and asked, but Ruiyun hadn't returned yet. The old nanny was chattering and making noise, but she stopped when she saw Zuo Shichen coming. Seeing that she couldn't bear it anymore, the old nanny walked to the pavilion first, saying to Zuo Shichen, "Second Young Master, come in and sit down. I have something to tell you." Zuo Shichen followed her in and sat on a sofa, waiting to hear what she had to say. It must be about Ruiyun. The old nanny said hesitantly, "It's okay to tell you, Second Young Master. Our girl is going to be promoted." Zuo Shichen was stunned. What does she mean by "promoted"? The "girl" she's talking about is, of course, Ruiyun. Officials have promotions, which are called "promotions." Are the people in the courtesan houses the same as the people who work?

Up 18.9 Qian from the Previous Day

Deviating from the Norm, Like Madness

The Market is Chaotic, Fluctuating by Ten Taels Frequently

Yesterday, the surge in the gold standard seemed like madness, soaring fiercely by about twenty taels, surpassing the new peak of over five hundred and ninety taels. However, the market was extremely chaotic, with fluctuations of ten taels being commonplace. In the morning session, there were discrepancies of more than twenty taels, and in the afternoon session, there were also reviews of ten taels. There were no large-scale entries or exits in the market. This excessive rise and fall made people extremely confused. Foreign exchange shrank greatly, and the quoted price decreased madly by seven-and-a-half gears, which was rare. The internal price was especially high, and banks had no intention of buying or selling, so only a few transactions were made. Among the firms, some bought to cover their positions, while Fuchang, Zhifeng, Yonghengxing, etc., all sold. After the large drop in the morning, the price soared, reaching the new high price of 598.5 taels. Afterwards, the price fluctuated, and there was no certainty. The storm was very strong. The Price of Geng Rice in Zhongguan Gradually Increases, and Foreign Rice Continues to Rise

Zhabei: Yesterday, about ten boats from various groups arrived, sales were average, and the price of high-quality North Geng rice remained unchanged, with the general price of top-grade rice opening at 21 yuan and 7 jiao, similar to the previous day. The price of Zhongguan white Geng rice gradually increased by half a jiao, due to the active consumption in this street. The situation is extremely good. The import and export of old Geng rice is quite large. The price of thin rice continues to tighten, opening high at 20 yuan. The buying interest from outside the customs is not weak. There are no goods arriving in Yangdu, Jianli Road for supply to Shanghai, and domestic rice merchants are completely focused on transporting foreign rice. Therefore, there are no goods being loaded and shipped, and they are hoping for supply of premium quality rice. As a result, the price of native premium rice has become stagnant. Due to the smooth sales, the price of foreign rice has risen by about 2 jiao, with high-quality goods above 18 yuan. The situation looks good. Although it rained all day, the trading was still strong.

South Shanghai: Only a few boats arrived from the river. Sales in the market are still acceptable. Shops in the villages and towns of Suzhou, Tongzhou, Changzhou, and Xixi are all purchasing. The market is rising again by one or two jiao. The price of ordinary rice is around 19 yuan and 5 jiao. According to recent reports, the price of Geng rice in the north and south markets seems to be highest at 20 yuan on the surface, but in reality, it mostly exceeds this amount. In the South Shanghai region, the arrival of thin early rice is scarce, and sales are picking up. Prices continue to rise, with good quality rice priced at more than one jiao. There is an intermittent supply of indica rice due to the lack of a standard market. The price of white rice is extremely sluggish. Due to the weak inventory and arrivals, the market is gradually firming up, approaching one jiao.

Flour Market Rises Sharply in the Heavy Rain

Silver and Money Brokers Suddenly Engage in Buying

Prices Rise More Than Two Fen for Each Month

Yesterday, the flour market rose even more sharply. Prices were surprisingly bullish after the opening both in the morning and afternoon. In the afternoon, during the first two trading sessions, due to heavy rain, silver and money brokers from outside the industry purchased forward contracts for flour, driving the price up to around 2 taels and 5 qian. However, the Wuxi brokers sold off their positions, so the price slightly retreated after the sharp rise. The closing prices were: June, up 1 fen 25; July, up 2 fen 75; August, up 2 fen 25; September, up 1 fen 7; October, up 3 fen; November, up 2 fen 25.

The Standard Price of New Wheat Fluctuates by One Qian Again

Yesterday, the wheat market opened with soaring prices for all months. During the afternoon session, due to the sharp rise in flour prices, more speculators outside the industry paid attention, and prices were even hotter. July and November both rose by a significant amount of 1 qian and 12 fen compared to the previous day. June, August, and September also rose by 8 or 9 fen. At the final close, June was up 2 fen, August was up 45 fen, September was up 2 fen, and October was up 6 fen. There were 700-800 bags of old wheat being offered, priced at 5 taels and 5 fen. New wheat arrivals were scarce, and the market sentiment was particularly good due to the rain. Nearly 1,000 bags were sold. Caishi wheat was priced at 4 taels and 7 qian 5 fen, Huzhou wheat at 4 taels and 6 qian 3 fen, and Jiading wheat at 4 taels and 5 qian 1 fen.

Sugar Market: Japanese Sugar Rises Sharply by Over Three Qian

National Sugar Opens with 2,000 Bags and Remains Popular

Yesterday, the sugar market received reports from the producing areas that the spot price of Cuban sugar remained at 1.375, New York sugar futures were 1.50 for September, 1.59 for December, and 1.68 for March next year, each up by 3 fen compared to the previous report. May was at 1.74, also up by 2 fen. The spot price of Javanese sugar was 10 guilders, a sharp increase of 3.75 compared to the previous price. June sugar futures were priced at 9.50, July at 9.375, each up by 1.25, and August at 9.125, down by 1.25. The initial trading price of crude granulated sugar, due to the rapid contraction of the exchange rate, was 7 taels and 6 qian, and trading was quite active. The price rose from 7 taels 6 qian 2 fen 5 li to 6 qian 5 fen. In the after market the price rose to 7 taels 7 qian, and the supply was scarce. The asking price was 7 taels 8 qian, but buyers hesitated slightly, so no transaction resulted. Fine granulated sugar was priced at 7 taels 7 qian to 8 qian, No. 20 medium granulated sugar at 7 taels 5 to 5 qian 5 fen, and No. 10 Dutch red sugar at 6 taels. The market was bullish. The rise in Japanese sugar was even more severe, jumping by more than 3 qian, with a strong momentum to rise even higher. The prices for Minghua YT were 8 taels 3 qian to 3 qian 5 fen, YP at 8 taels 4 qian 5 fen to 5 qian, and YRO at 7 qian 9 qian to 8 taels. All of these were popular. Only Taikoo Sugar B remained, with the asking price at 8 yuan and 8 jiao in Hong Kong dollars, up 3 jiao compared to the previous price, but no one was asking about it. National Sugar opened with 2,000 bags of Zhen brand, priced at 8 taels and 3 qian, and Shi brand at 8 taels. The market sentiment was still popular. The Shanghai and China No. 2 factories, which are also under the National Sugar banner, increased their prices by 2 qian, with the Ren and Zhong brands both priced at 10 taels and 4 qian, and the Qian and Hua brands both priced at 10 taels and 2 qian. The market situation was quite firm. The two factories are tightening their sales because the spot price of raw sugar has risen sharply.

Drastic Changes in Silk Exchange Rate Make Tea Market Even More Quiet

Yesterday, the tea market in Shanghai was even quieter. There were no transactions for green tea from Tunxi and Suian. There were also no large transactions for Qimen black tea. High-grade black tea has already become scarce. The British market is not in urgent need of medium and low-grade goods. In addition, the price of gold has risen sharply and the exchange rate has fluctuated drastically. Therefore, most merchants are adopting a wait-and-see attitude.

Spring Chinese Silk Exports to the US are Slightly Stronger

Eight Thousand Plus Packs in Jan-Feb, Over Ten Thousand in March

Chinese silk is the largest export trade, especially sales to the United States. The monthly export volume to the United States is mostly as high as four or five thousand packs, and no less than two or three thousand packs. This spring, because the US government has set a deadline of May 1 to impose import silk taxes, and silver prices are also cheap (Chinese silk trade is valued in taels), and the Japanese silver price is slowly rising, so American silk merchants are abandoning Japanese silk in favour of the processing of Chinese silk. American firms are actively transporting their existing stocks to the United States, so exports are more active. According to statistics, the export of Chinese silk to the United States in January was 8,708 packs, in February 8,221 packs, and in March 10,551 packs. During the same period last year, they were only more than 4,000 to 5,000 packs.
